###################################
#
# Anglo Saxon Invasion Events
#
# Id 313000 - 313199
#
###################################
#
# 313000 - 313005	Anglian Invasions
# 313006 - 313019 	North Angle Invasions
# 313020 - 313020	South Saxon Invasions
# 313021 - 313029	West Saxon Invasions
# 313030 - 313049 	Rise of Lindsey
# 313050 - 313059	Iclingas/Mercian Invasions
# 313060 - 313069	Hwiccian Invasions
# 313070 - 313076	Rise of the Iclingas
# 313077 - 313079	Rise of Mercia (generic)
# 313080 - 313089	Rise of Cantia
# 313090 - 313099	Decline of Sussex
# 313100 - 313119	Collapse of Anglia
# 313120 - 313129	Rise of Bernicia
# 313130 - 313139	Rise of Deira
# 313150 - 313169	Return of the Saxons
# 313170 - 313178	Anglia/Sussex province-granting events
# 313179 - 313179   Conquest of Magnis
# 313180 - 313192	Revolts for New Kingdoms
# 313197 - 313199	Dynasties and Family Branches

### ANGLIAN INVASIONS ###

# Anglian Invasions 480 - 484 AD, Causennae, Ciniubantum, and Durocobrivis
narrative_event = {
	id = 313000
	title = "EVTNAME313000"
	desc = "EVTDESC313000"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_saxon_army"
	
	only_rulers = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	ai = yes
	
	trigger = {
		year = 480
		has_landed_title = k_anglia
		48 = {	# Thunreslea
			owner = {
				realm = {								
					OR = { 
						title = e_aengland
						title = k_anglia
					}
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			c_causennae = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
			c_ciniubantum = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
			c_durocobrivis = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
		}
		top_liege = { ai = yes }
		is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		OR = {
			religion = germanic_pagan
			religion = germanic_pagan_reformed
		}
		war = no
		NOT = { has_global_flag = anglian_invasion_480 }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = anglia_collapse_start }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = anglia_collapsed }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 482
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 483
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 484
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			c_causennae = { has_truce_with_owner_trigger = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			c_ciniubantum = { has_truce_with_owner_trigger = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			c_durocobrivis = { has_truce_with_owner_trigger = yes }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { set_global_flag = anglian_invasion_480 }
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
		trigger = {
			ai = yes
			has_landed_title = k_anglia
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_causennae = {
					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			c_causennae = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_ciniubantum = {
					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			c_ciniubantum = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_durocobrivis = {
					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			c_durocobrivis = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		create_character = {
			random_traits = yes
			dynasty = random
			religion = germanic_pagan
			culture = angle
			female = no
			age = 35
			attributes = {
				martial = 11
			}
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
		}
		new_character = {
			spawn_unit = {
				province = 48 # Thunreslea
				troops =
				{
					light_infantry = { 550 550 }
					heavy_infantry = { 250 250 }
					pikemen = { 300 300 }
					archers = { 100 100 }
				}
				attrition = 0.5
			}
			spawn_unit = {
				province = 48 # Thunreslea
				troops =
				{
					light_infantry = { 600 600 }
					heavy_infantry = { 350 350 }
					pikemen = { 450 450 }
					archers = { 300 300 }
				}
				attrition = 0.25
				disband_on_peace = yes
			}
			spawn_unit = {
				province = 48 # Thunreslea
				troops =
				{
					light_infantry = { 500 500 }
					heavy_infantry = { 650 650 }
					pikemen = { 450 450 }
					archers = { 500 500 }
				}
				attrition = 0.25
				disband_on_peace = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313000"	# Other Saxons
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
			NOT = { has_landed_title = k_anglia }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313000"	# Britons
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture = briton
				culture = romanobritish
				culture = cumbrian
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC313000"	# Others
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
			NOT = { culture = briton }
			NOT = { culture = romanobritish }
			NOT = { culture = cumbrian }
		}
	}
}
# Anglian Invasions 485 - 489 AD, Gwash and Verulanium
narrative_event = {
	id = 313001
	title = "EVTNAME313001"
	desc = "EVTDESC313001"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_saxon_army"
	
	only_rulers = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		year = 485
		had_global_flag = { flag = anglian_invasion_480 days = 365 }
		war = no
		has_landed_title = k_anglia
		48 = {	# Thunreslea
			owner = {
				realm = {								
					OR = { 
						title = e_aengland
						title = k_anglia
					}
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			c_verulanium = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
			c_gwash = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
		}
		is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		OR = {
			religion = germanic_pagan
			religion = germanic_pagan_reformed
		}
		ai = yes
		top_liege = { ai = yes }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = anglian_invasion_485 }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 486
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 487
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 488
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			c_verulanium = { has_truce_with_owner_trigger = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			c_gwash = { has_truce_with_owner_trigger = yes }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { set_global_flag = anglian_invasion_485 }
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
		trigger = {
			ai = yes
			has_landed_title = k_anglia
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_verulanium = {
					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			c_verulanium = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_gwash = {
					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			add_claim = c_gwash
			c_gwash = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		create_character = {
			random_traits = yes
			dynasty = random
			religion = germanic_pagan
			culture = angle
			female = no
			age = 32
			attributes = {
				martial = 10
			}
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
		}
		new_character = {
			spawn_unit = {
				province = 48 # Thunreslea
				troops = {
					light_infantry = { 200 200 }
					heavy_infantry = { 150 150 }
					pikemen = { 150 150 }
				}
				attrition = 1
			}
			spawn_unit = {
				province = 48 # Thunreslea
				troops = {
					light_infantry = { 300 300 }
					heavy_infantry = { 250 250 }
					pikemen = { 200 200 }
					archers = { 100 100 }
				}
				disband_on_peace = yes
				attrition = 0.5
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { NOT = { completely_controls = c_durocobrivis } } }
				spawn_unit = {
					province = 48 # Thunreslea
					troops = {
						light_infantry = { 300 300 }
						heavy_infantry = { 150 150 }
						pikemen = { 200 200 }
						archers = { 100 100 }
					}
					disband_on_peace = yes
					attrition = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313001"	# Other Saxons
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
			NOT = { has_landed_title = k_anglia }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313001"	# Britons
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture = briton
				culture = romanobritish
				culture = cumbrian
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC313001"	# Others
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
			NOT = { culture = briton }
			NOT = { culture = romanobritish }
			NOT = { culture = cumbrian }
		}
	}
}
# Anglian Invasions 490 - 495 AD (all previous provinces if not conquered, Margidunum, Latimer)
narrative_event = {
	id = 313002
	title = "EVTNAME313002"
	desc = "EVTDESC313002"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_saxon_army_banners"
	
	only_rulers = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		year = 490
		war = no
		had_global_flag = { flag = anglian_invasion_485 days = 365 }
		has_landed_title = k_anglia
		48 = {	# Thunreslea
			owner = {
				realm = {								
					OR = { 
						title = e_aengland
						title = k_anglia
					}
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			c_chiltern_hills = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
			c_causennae = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
			c_verulanium = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
			c_durocobrivis = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
			c_ciniubantum = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
			c_gwash = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
			c_margidunum = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
		}
		ai = yes
		top_liege = { ai = yes }
		is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		OR = {
			religion = germanic_pagan
			religion = germanic_pagan_reformed
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = anglian_invasion_490 }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 491
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 492
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 493
		}
		modifier = {			# If one of the previous conquests failed
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				c_causennae = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
				c_verulanium = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
				c_durocobrivis = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
				c_ciniubantum = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
				c_gwash = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			c_margidunum = { has_truce_with_owner_trigger = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			c_chiltern_hills = { has_truce_with_owner_trigger = yes }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { set_global_flag = anglian_invasion_490 }
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
		trigger = {
			ai = yes
			has_landed_title = k_anglia
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_causennae = {
					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			c_causennae = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_ciniubantum = {
					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			c_ciniubantum = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_durocobrivis = {
					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			c_durocobrivis = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_verulanium = {
					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			c_verulanium = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_gwash = {
					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			c_gwash = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_chiltern_hills = {
					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			c_chiltern_hills = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_margidunum = {
					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			c_margidunum = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		spawn_unit = {
			province = 48 # Thunreslea
			troops = {	
				light_infantry = { 250 250 }
				heavy_infantry = { 150 150 }
				pikemen = { 75 75 }
			}
			attrition = 1
		}
		spawn_unit = {
			province = 48 # Thunreslea
			troops = {	
				light_infantry = { 300 300 }
				heavy_infantry = { 350 350 }
				pikemen = { 150 150 }
				archers = { 100 100 }
			}
			attrition = 1
			disband_on_peace = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NAND = {
					completely_controls = c_causennae
					completely_controls = c_gwash
					completely_controls = c_durocobrivis
					completely_controls = c_verulanium
					completely_controls = c_ciniubantum
				}
			}
			create_character = {
				random_traits = yes
				dynasty = random
				religion = germanic_pagan
				culture = angle
				female = no
				age = 36
				attributes = {
					martial = 11
				}
				trait = brilliant_strategist
				trait = veteran
				trait = brave
			}
			new_character = {
				spawn_unit = {
					province = 48 # Thunreslea
					troops = {	
						light_infantry = { 550 550 }
						heavy_infantry = { 350 350 }
						pikemen = { 250 250 }
					}
					attrition = 1
				}
				spawn_unit = {
					province = 48 # Thunreslea
					troops = {	
						light_infantry = { 650 650 }
						heavy_infantry = { 450 450 }
						pikemen = { 200 200 }
						archers = { 150 150 }
					}
					attrition = 1
					disband_on_peace = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313002"	# Other Saxons
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
			NOT = { has_landed_title = k_anglia }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313002"	# Britons
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture = briton
				culture = romanobritish
				culture = cumbrian
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC313002"	# Others
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
			NOT = { culture = briton }
			NOT = { culture = romanobritish }
			NOT = { culture = cumbrian }
		}
	}
}
# Anglian Invasions 496 - 500 AD, Ratae, Magiovinium, Lactodorum (with checks for Margidunum and Latimer) 
narrative_event = {
	id = 313003
	title = "EVTNAME313003"
	desc = "EVTDESC313003"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_ship_cloudy_sunset"
	
	only_rulers = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		year = 496
		had_global_flag = { flag = anglian_invasion_490 days = 365 }
		war = no
		has_landed_title = k_anglia
		48 = {	# Thunreslea
			owner = {
				realm = {								
					OR = { 
						title = e_aengland
						title = k_anglia
					}
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			c_lactodorum = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
			c_magiovinium = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
			c_margidunum = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
			c_chiltern_hills = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
			c_ratae = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
		}
		ai = yes
		top_liege = { ai = yes }
		is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		OR = {
			religion = germanic_pagan
			religion = germanic_pagan_reformed
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = anglian_invasion_496 }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24

			factor = 0.5
			year = 497
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 498
		}

			factor = 0.5
			year = 499
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			c_margidunum = { has_truce_with_owner_trigger = yes }
		}

		}

			c_magiovinium = { has_truce_with_owner_trigger = yes }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { set_global_flag = anglian_invasion_496 }

					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			c_margidunum = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_ratae = {
					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			c_ratae = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_lactodorum = {
					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			c_lactodorum = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_chiltern_hills = {
					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			c_chiltern_hills = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_magiovinium = {
					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			c_magiovinium = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313003"	# Other Saxons
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
			NOT = { has_landed_title = k_anglia }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313003"	# Britons
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture = briton
				culture = romanobritish
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC313003"	# Others
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
			NOT = { culture = briton }
			NOT = { culture = romanobritish }
		}
	}
}
# Anglian Invasions 501 - 505 AD, Bannaventa and Ad Pontem (with checks for Ratae and Magiovinium)
narrative_event = {
	id = 313004
	title = "EVTNAME313004"
	desc = "EVTDESC313004"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_saxon_army"
	
	only_rulers = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no

		year = 501

		has_landed_title = k_anglia
		48 = {	# Thunreslea
			owner = {
				realm = {								
					OR = { 
						title = e_aengland
						title = k_anglia
					}
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			c_bannaventa = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
			c_ad_pontem = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
			c_magiovinium = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
			c_ratae = { can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes }
		}
		ai = yes
		top_liege = { ai = yes }

	}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 502
		}

			year = 503
		}

			factor = 0.5
			year = 504
		}
		modifier = {

			c_bannaventa = { has_truce_with_owner_trigger = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			c_ad_pontem = { has_truce_with_owner_trigger = yes }
		}
	}

					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_bannaventa = {
					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			c_bannaventa = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_ad_pontem = {
					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			c_ad_pontem = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_magiovinium = {
					can_conquer_anglosaxon_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			c_magiovinium = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313004"	# Other Saxons

## BERNICIAN REVOLT

# Angles of Bernicia give ultimatum
character_event = {
	id = 313120
	title = "EVTNAME313120"
	desc = "EVTDESC313120"
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_warships"
	
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_character_flag = angle_sending_ultimatum
			AND = {
				ai = yes		# Human player triggers by decision
				year = 540
				NOT = { year = 580 }
				war = no
				is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
				has_landed_title = d_north_angles
				trait = foederate
				OR = {
					AND = {
						independent = no
						liege = {
							culture_group = celtic
						}
					}
					AND = {
						is_tributary = { type = foederati }
						suzerain = {
							culture_group = celtic
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = angles_bernicia_ultimatum }
					had_global_flag =  { flag = angles_bernicia_ultimatum days = 3650 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			year = 545
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 550
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			year = 560
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			year = 570
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			d_deira = { has_holder = yes }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = angle_sending_ultimatum
		set_global_flag = angles_bernicia_ultimatum
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313120"	# Send Ultimatum
		ai_chance = { factor = 95 }
		if = {
			limit = { independent = no }
			liege = {
				character_event = {	id = 313121 days = 1 }
			}
			break = yes
		}
		suzerain = {
			character_event = {	id = 313121 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313120"	# Don't send ultimatum
		trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 5 
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOR = {
					trait = loyal
					trait = content
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					trait = unloyal
					trait = ambitious 
				}
			}
		}
		prestige = -100
	}
}

# Liege receives ultimatum
character_event = {
	id = 313121
	title = "EVTNAME313121"
	desc = "EVTDESC313121"
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_emissary"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { independent = no }
			liege = { save_event_target_as = bryneich_liege }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313121"	# Accept Ultimatum
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 20 
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				top_liege = {
					NOT = { num_of_count_titles_in_realm = 2 }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				top_liege = {
					num_of_count_titles_in_realm = 4
				}
			}
		}
		prestige = -200
		FROM = {
			character_event = {	id = 313122 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313121"	# Refuse ultimatum
		ai_chance = { factor = 80 }
		prestige = 100
		FROM = {
			character_event = {	id = 313124 days = 1 }
		}
		set_character_flag = bernicia_proper_liege
	}
}

# Ultimatum Accepted
character_event = {
	id = 313122
	title = EVTNAME313122
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_saxon_army_banners"
	
	major = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# Victorious Angles
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313122
		trigger = {
			character = ROOT
		}
	}
	
	# Former ruler of Bryneich
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313122_1
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
	}
	
	# Bryneich liege, if there is one
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313122_2
		trigger = {
			event_target:bryneich_liege = {
				character = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Other Anglo-Saxons
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313122_3
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				character = ROOT
				character = FROM
				event_target:bryneich_liege = {
					character = PREV
				}
			}
			culture_group = germanic
			is_romanized_germanic_trigger = no
		}
	}
	
	# Other Britons
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313122_4
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				character = ROOT
				character = FROM
				event_target:bryneich_liege = {
					character = PREV
				}
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { culture_group = germanic }
				is_romanized_germanic_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	major_trigger = {
		OR = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
			is_brythonic_culture_trigger = yes
			capital_scope = {
				region = world_britannia
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { independent = yes }
			suzerain = {
				save_event_target_as = former_liege
			}
			break = yes
		}
		liege = {
			save_event_target_as = former_liege
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313122"
		trigger = {
			character = ROOT
		}
		prestige = 200
		event_target:former_liege = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_landed_title = k_bryneich
					num_of_king_titles = 1
					tier = KING
				}
				any_vassal = {
					limit = { tier = COUNT }
					set_character_flag = bernicia_vassal
				}
				set_character_flag = bernicia_vassal
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						num_of_king_titles = 2
						tier = EMPEROR
						NOT = { has_landed_title = k_bryneich }
					}
				}
				any_province = {
					limit = { region = custom_bernicia }
					county = {
						holder_scope = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									num_of_count_titles = 1
									tier = COUNT
									same_realm = FROM
								}
								set_character_flag = bernicia_vassal
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = {
										OR = {
											num_of_count_titles = 1
											tier = COUNT
										}
									}
									same_realm = FROM
								}
								PREV = { grant_title = ROOT }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_old_tyne = {
					holder_scope = {
						same_realm = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			c_old_tyne = {
				grant_title = ROOT
				hidden_tooltip = {
					location = {
						province_event = {
							id = 55002
							days = 365
							random = 100
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		d_bernicia = { grant_title = ROOT }
		k_bryneich = { destroy_landed_title = k_bryneich }
		d_eastrheged = { destroy_landed_title = d_eastrheged }
		d_bryneich = { destroy_landed_title = d_bryneich }
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = bernicia_vassal }
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
			clr_character_flag = bernicia_vassal
		}
		set_defacto_liege = THIS
		any_realm_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = anglosaxon_settlement }
			remove_province_modifier = anglosaxon_settlement
		}
		capital_scope = {
			ROOT = {
				create_character = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = random
					religion = germanic_pagan
					culture = angle
					female = no
					age = 28
					attributes = {
						martial = 11
					}
					trait = brilliant_strategist
					trait = veteran
					trait = diligent
					trait = skilled_warrior
				}
				new_character = {
					spawn_unit = {
						province = PREVPREV 
						troops = {
							light_infantry = { 800 800 }
							heavy_infantry = { 500 500 }
							pikemen = { 350 350 }
							archers = { 200 200 }
						}
						attrition = 1
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { ai = yes } }
						spawn_unit = {
							province = PREVPREV 
							troops = {
								light_infantry = { 400 400 }
								heavy_infantry = { 300 300 }
								pikemen = { 250 250 }
								archers = { 150 150 }
							}
							attrition = 0.5
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		name = "EVTOPTB313122"
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:bryneich_liege = {
				character = PREV
			}
		}
		name = "EVTOPTC313122"
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				character = ROOT
				character = FROM
				event_target:bryneich_liege = {
					character = PREV
				}
			}
			culture_group = germanic
			is_romanized_germanic_trigger = no
		}
		name = "EVTOPTD313122"
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				character = ROOT
				character = FROM
				event_target:bryneich_liege = {
					character = PREV
				}
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { culture_group = germanic }
				is_romanized_germanic_trigger = yes
			}
			NOT = { trait = foederate_employer }
		}
		name = "EVTOPTC313122"
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				character = ROOT
				character = FROM
				event_target:bryneich_liege = {
					character = PREV
				}
			}

# Ultimatum Refused
character_event = {
	id = 313124
	title = "EVTNAME313124"
	desc = "EVTDESC313124"
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_emissary"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313124"	# Go to war
		prestige = 200
		if = {
			limit = { independent = no }
			set_defacto_liege = THIS
		}
		if = {
			limit = { independent = yes }
			suzerain = {
				remove_tributary = ROOT
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = foederate_revolt
		set_character_flag = foederate_revolt_bernicia
		capital_scope = {
			ROOT = {
				create_character = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = random
					religion = germanic_pagan
					culture = angle
					female = no
					age = 30
					attributes = {
						martial = 10
					}
					trait = brilliant_strategist
					trait = veteran
					trait = brave
					trait = skilled_warrior
				}
				new_character = {
					spawn_unit = {
						province = PREVPREV
						troops = {
							light_infantry = { 400 400 }
							heavy_infantry = { 350 350 }
							pikemen = { 250 250 }
							archers = { 150 150 }
						}
						attrition = 0.5
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { ai = yes } }
						spawn_unit = {
							province = PREVPREV
							troops = {
								light_infantry = { 500 500 }
								heavy_infantry = { 350 350 }
								pikemen = { 350 350 }
								archers = { 200 200 }
							}
							attrition = 0.5
						}
					}
					spawn_unit = {
						province = PREVPREV
						troops = {
							light_infantry = { 600 600 }
							heavy_infantry = { 500 500 }
							pikemen = { 350 350 }
							archers = { 350 350 }
						}
						attrition = 0.5
						disband_on_peace = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_old_tyne = {
					holder_scope = {
						OR = {
							character = FROM
							any_liege = {
								character = FROM
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							character = ROOT
							any_liege = {
								character = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			c_old_tyne = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				war = no
				c_medcaut = {
					holder_scope = {
						OR = {
							character = FROM
							any_liege = {
								character = FROM
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							character = ROOT
							any_liege = {
								character = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			c_medcaut = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				war = no
			}
			random_province = {
				limit = { 
					region = custom_bernicia
					owner = {
						OR = {
							character = FROM
							any_liege = {
								character = FROM
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							character = ROOT
							any_liege = {
								character = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								character = ROOT
								any_liege = {
									character = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				county = {
					reverse_war = {
						target = ROOT
						casus_belli = county_conquest
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {	id = 313126 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313124"	# Back down
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		prestige = -200
		FROM = {
			character_event = {	id = 313127 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

# Northern Invasions 547 AD, settlers land on Bernicia (1st Invasion)
province_event = {
	id = 313006
	title = "EVTNAME313006"
	desc = "EVTDESC313006"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_anglosaxons_ashore"
	
	trigger = {
		province_id = 68	# Bernicia
		year = 547
		NOT = { year = 580 }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = anglian_north_invasion_547 }
		d_north_angles = { has_holder = no }
		owner = {
			top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 60
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.05
			c_bernicia = {
				holder_scope = {

							independent = yes
							lower_tier_than = KING
						}
						top_liege = {
							lower_tier_than = KING
						}
						war = yes
					}
				}
			}					
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 552
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 560
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 565
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = anglian_north_invasion_547	
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					c_benoc_folc = { has_holder = no }
					has_global_flag = benoc_folc_migrated_bernicia
				}
			}
			create_character = {
				random_traits = no
				name = "Eoppa"
				dynasty = 662
				religion = germanic_pagan
				culture = angle
				employer = d_north_angles

					martial = 8
					diplomacy = 7
					stewardship = 6

				}

				trait = lustful
				trait = just
			}
			new_character = {
				dynasty = 662
				set_character_flag = eoppa_of_bernicia
				save_global_event_target_as = initial_north_angle_leader
				set_character_flag = bernicia_invader
				d_north_angles = {
					activate_title = { title = d_north_angles status = yes }
					gain_title = PREV
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = high_tribal_government } }
					set_government_type = high_tribal_government
				}
				d_bernicia = {
					add_claim = PREV
				}

					add_claim = PREV
				}

					add_claim = PREV
				}
				c_medcaut = {
					add_claim = PREV
				}
				character_event = { id = 313007 }
				character_event = { id = 313016 }
				wealth = 200
				prestige = 500
				create_character = {
					name="Glædwine"
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = 300
					religion = germanic_pagan
					culture = angle
					female = no
					employer = d_north_angles
					age = 36
					attributes = {
						martial = 7
						stewardship = 8
						diplomacy = 6
					}
					trait = brilliant_strategist
					trait = war_hero
					trait = brave
					trait = loyal
					trait = heavy_infantry_leader
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = eoppa_created
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_benoc_folc = { has_holder = yes }
				NOT = { has_global_flag = benoc_folc_migrated_bernicia }
			}
			c_benoc_folc = {
				holder_scope = {
					set_character_flag = bernicia_invader
					d_north_angles = {
						activate_title = { title = d_north_angles status = yes }
						gain_title = PREV
					}
					set_defacto_liege = THIS
					set_government_type = high_tribal_government
					d_bernicia = {
						add_claim = PREV
					}
					c_bernicia = {
						add_claim = PREV
					}
					c_old_tyne = {
						add_claim = PREV
					}
					c_medcaut = {
						add_claim = PREV
					}
					character_event = { id = 313007 }
					wealth = 100
					prestige = 200
					create_character = {
						name="Glædwine"
						random_traits = yes
						dynasty = 300
						religion = germanic_pagan
						culture = angle
						female = no
						employer = d_north_angles
						age = 36
						attributes = {
							martial = 7
							stewardship = 8

						}

						trait = war_hero
						trait = brave
						trait = loyal

					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						save_global_event_target_as = initial_north_angle_leader
						c_benoc_folc = {
							destroy_landless_count_level_title_effect = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313006"
		trigger = {
			has_landed_title = c_benoc_folc
			NOT = { has_global_flag = benoc_folc_migrated_bernicia }

	trigger = {
		province_id = 68	# Bernicia
		has_global_flag = anglian_north_invasion_547
		NOT = { has_province_flag = anglian_invasion }
		NOT = { culture = angle }
		owner = { culture = angle }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_province_flag = anglian_invasion
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA3130079"
		culture = angle
		religion = germanic_pagan
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = depopulated_1
			}
			remove_province_modifier = depopulated_1
			clr_province_flag = angeln_depopulation
			clr_province_flag = southern_britain_depopulation
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = depopulated_2
			}
			remove_province_modifier = depopulated_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = depopulated_3
			}
			remove_province_modifier = depopulated_3
		}
	}
}

# Maintain effort
character_event = {
	id = 313009
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	
	only_rulers = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		#has_global_flag = anglian_north_invasion_547
		year = 545
		independent = yes
		NOT = { trait = foederate }
		OR = {
			has_landed_title = d_north_angles
			AND = {
				has_character_flag = bernicia_invader
				d_north_angles = { has_holder = no }
			}
		}
		war = no
		prestige = 75
		wealth = 25
		any_realm_province = {
			any_neighbor_province = {
				region = custom_bernicia
				ROOT_can_declare_war_against_province_trigger = yes
			}
		}			
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 6
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			realm_size = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			realm_size = 6
		}
	}
		
	option = {
		name = "OK"
		random_province = {			# Try to conquer coastal provinces first
			limit = {
				region = custom_bernicia
				ROOT_can_declare_war_against_province_trigger = yes
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { top_liege = { character = ROOT } }
				}
				any_neighbor_province = {
					is_land = no
				}
			}
			county = {
				declare_conquest_war = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { war = no }
			random_province = {	
				limit = {
					region = custom_bernicia
					ROOT_can_declare_war_against_province_trigger = yes
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = { top_liege = { character = ROOT } }
					}
				}
				county = {
					declare_conquest_war = yes
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { war = yes	}
			capital_scope = {
				ROOT = {
					spawn_unit = {
						province = PREV
						home = PREV
						owner = ROOT
						troops = {
							light_infantry = { 600 600 }
							pikemen = { 450 450 }
							heavy_infantry = { 450 450 }
							archers = { 500 500 }
						}
						attrition = 0.5
					}
					spawn_unit = {
						province = PREV
						home = PREV
						owner = ROOT
						troops = {
							light_infantry = { 500 500 }
							pikemen = { 450 450 }
							heavy_infantry = { 350 350 }
							archers = { 450 450 }
						}
						attrition = 0.5
						disband_on_peace = yes
					}
					wealth = 50
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Disband Anglo-Saxon invasion titles if defeated
character_event = {
	id = 313013
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	only_rulers = yes
	#ai = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_landed_title = d_north_angles
			has_landed_title = d_west_saxons
			has_landed_title = d_angles
			has_landed_title = d_iclingas
			has_landed_title = d_hwiccas
			has_landed_title = d_saxon_hamaland
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				war = no
				is_landed = no
			}
			any_demesne_title = {
				higher_tier_than = COUNT
				is_titular = no 
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_landed_title = d_north_angles }
			d_north_angles = { unsafe_destroy_landed_title = d_north_angles }
			activate_title = { title = d_north_angles status = no }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_landed_title = d_angles }
			d_angles = { unsafe_destroy_landed_title = d_angles }
			activate_title = { title = d_angles status = no }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_landed_title = d_west_saxons }
			d_west_saxons = { unsafe_destroy_landed_title = d_west_saxons }
			any_province = {
				clr_province_flag = west_saxon_invasion_province
			}
			activate_title = { title = d_west_saxons status = no }
			if = {
				limit = { is_landed = no }
				clr_global_flag = west_saxon_invasion_hampshire
				clr_global_flag = west_saxon_invasion_dorset
				clr_global_flag = west_saxon_invasion_berkshire
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_landed_title = d_iclingas }
			d_iclingas = { unsafe_destroy_landed_title = THIS }
			activate_title = { title = d_iclingas status = no }
			if = {
				limit = { is_landed = no }
				clr_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_middle_anglia
				clr_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_pegansaete
				clr_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_tomsaete
				clr_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_grentbryce
				clr_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_wrocensaete
				clr_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_magonsaete
				clr_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_cilternsaete
				clr_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_hwicce
				any_province = {
					clr_province_flag = iclingas_target_county
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_landed_title = d_hwiccas }
			d_hwiccas = { unsafe_destroy_landed_title = d_hwiccas }
			activate_title = { title = d_hwiccas status = no }
			if = {
				limit = { is_landed = no }
				clr_global_flag = hwiccas_invasion_hwicce
				clr_global_flag = hwiccas_invasion_cilternsaete
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_landed_title = d_saxon_hamaland }
			d_saxon_hamaland = { unsafe_destroy_landed_title = d_saxon_hamaland }
			activate_title = { title = d_saxon_hamaland status = no }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
	}
}		
	
# Inheritance of invader flags
character_event = {
	id = 313015
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROMFROM = {
			OR = {
				has_character_flag = bernicia_invader
				has_character_flag = anglia_invader
				has_character_flag = wessex_invader
				has_character_flag = mercia_invader
				has_character_flag = hwicce_invader
				has_character_flag = hamaland_invader
				has_character_flag = saxon_gallic_invader
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { FROMFROM = { has_character_flag = bernicia_invader } }
			set_character_flag = bernicia_invader
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROMFROM = { has_character_flag = anglia_invader } }
			set_character_flag = anglia_invader
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROMFROM = { has_character_flag = wessex_invader } }
			set_character_flag = wessex_invader
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROMFROM = { has_character_flag = mercia_invader } }
			set_character_flag = mercia_invader
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:mercia_invader = {
					FROMFROM = { 
						character = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = mercia_invader
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROMFROM = { has_character_flag = hwicce_invader } }
			set_character_flag = hwicce_invader
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:hwicce_invader = {
					FROMFROM = { 
						character = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = hwicce_invader
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROMFROM = { has_character_flag = hamaland_invader } }
			set_character_flag = hamaland_invader
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROMFROM = { has_character_flag = saxon_gallic_invader } }
			set_character_flag = saxon_gallic_invader
		}		
	}
}

# Clear invader flags from unlanded characters

	id = 313018
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	
	ai = yes
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		OR = {
			has_character_flag = bernicia_invader
			has_character_flag = anglia_invader
			has_character_flag = wessex_invader
			has_character_flag = mercia_invader
			has_character_flag = hwicce_invader
			has_character_flag = hamaland_invader
			event_target:mercia_invader = {
				character = ROOT
			}
			event_target:hwicce_invader = {
				character = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = bernicia_invader
		clr_character_flag = anglia_invader
		clr_character_flag = wessex_invader
		clr_character_flag = mercia_invader
		clr_character_flag = hwicce_invader
		clr_character_flag = hamaland_invader
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:mercia_invader = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			clear_global_event_target = mercia_invader
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:hwicce_invader = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			clear_global_event_target = hwicce_invader
		}
	}
}

### RISE OF DEIRA ###

# Angles of Deira give ultimatum
character_event = {
	id = 313130
	title = "EVTNAME313130"
	desc = "EVTDESC313130"
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_warships"
	
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_character_flag = angle_sending_ultimatum
			AND = {
				ai = yes		# Human player triggers by decision
				year = 550
				NOT = { year = 580 }
				war = no
				is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
				has_landed_title = c_petuaria
				c_petuaria = {
					location = {
						is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
						has_province_modifier = anglosaxon_settlement
					}
				}
				trait = foederate
				OR = {
					AND = {
						independent = no
						liege = {
							culture_group = celtic
						}
					}
					AND = {
						is_tributary = { type = foederati }
						suzerain = {
							culture_group = celtic
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = angles_deira_ultimatum }
					had_global_flag =  { flag = angles_deira_ultimatum days = 3650 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 180
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			year = 555
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 560
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			year = 570
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			year = 580
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			d_bernicia = { has_holder = yes }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = angle_sending_ultimatum
		set_global_flag = angles_deira_ultimatum
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313130"	# Send Ultimatum
		ai_chance = { factor = 95 }
		if = {
			limit = { independent = no }
			liege = {
				character_event = {	id = 313131 days = 1 }
			}
			break = yes
		}
		suzerain = {
			character_event = {	id = 313131 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313130"	# Don't send ultimatum
		trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 5 
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOR = {
					trait = loyal
					trait = content
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					trait = unloyal
					trait = ambitious 
				}
			}
		}
		prestige = -100
	}
}

# Liege receives ultimatum
character_event = {
	id = 313131
	title = "EVTNAME313131"
	desc = "EVTDESC313131"
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_emissary"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { independent = no }
			liege = { save_event_target_as = ebrauc_liege }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313131"	# Accept Ultimatum
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 20 
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				top_liege = {
					NOT = { num_of_count_titles_in_realm = 2 }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				top_liege = {
					num_of_count_titles_in_realm = 4
				}
			}
		}
		prestige = -200
		FROM = {
			character_event = {	id = 313132 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313131"	# Refuse ultimatum
		ai_chance = { factor = 80 }
		prestige = 100
		FROM = {
			character_event = {	id = 313134 days = 1 }
		}
		set_character_flag = deira_proper_liege
	}
}

# Ultimatum Refused
character_event = {
	id = 313134
	title = "EVTNAME313134"
	desc = "EVTDESC313134"
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_emissary"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313134"	# Go to war
		prestige = 200
		if = {
			limit = { independent = no }
			set_defacto_liege = THIS
		}
		if = {
			limit = { independent = yes }
			suzerain = {
				remove_tributary = ROOT
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = foederate_revolt
		set_character_flag = foederate_revolt_deira
		capital_scope = {
			ROOT = {
				spawn_unit = {
					province = PREV
					troops = {
						light_infantry = { 800 800 }
						heavy_infantry = { 500 500 }
						pikemen = { 500 500 }
					}
					attrition = 1
				}
				create_character = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = random
					religion = germanic_pagan
					culture = angle
					female = no
					age = 30
					attributes = {
						martial = 10
					}
					trait = brilliant_strategist
					trait = veteran
					trait = brave
					trait = skilled_warrior
				}
				new_character = {
					spawn_unit = {
						province = PREVPREV
						troops = {
							light_infantry = { 350 750 }
							heavy_infantry = { 300 300 }
							pikemen = { 250 250 }
							archers = { 150 150 }
						}
						attrition = 0.5
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { ai = yes } }
						spawn_unit = {
							province = PREVPREV
							troops = {
								light_infantry = { 400 400 }
								heavy_infantry = { 300 300 }
								pikemen = { 300 300 }
								archers = { 100 100 }
							}
							attrition = 0.5
						}
					}
					spawn_unit = {
						province = PREVPREV
						troops = {
							light_infantry = { 650 650 }
							heavy_infantry = { 550 550 }
							pikemen = { 350 350 }
							archers = { 350 350 }
						}
						attrition = 0.5
						disband_on_peace = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_delgovicia = {
					holder_scope = {
						OR = {
							character = FROM
							any_liege = {
								character = FROM
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							character = ROOT
							any_liege = {
								character = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			c_delgovicia = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = county_conquest
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				war = no
			}
			random_province = {
				limit = { 
					region = custom_deira
					owner = {
						OR = {
							character = FROM
							any_liege = {
								character = FROM
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							character = ROOT
							any_liege = {
								character = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								character = ROOT
								any_liege = {
									character = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				county = {
					reverse_war = {
						target = ROOT
						casus_belli = county_conquest
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {	id = 313136 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313134"	# Back down
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		prestige = -200
		FROM = {
			character_event = {	id = 313137 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

# Maintain effort - Deira
character_event = {
	id = 313138
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	
	only_playable = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		lower_tier_than = KING
		OR = {
			has_landed_title = d_deira
			AND = {
				has_landed_title = d_bernicia
				year = 580
				d_deira = { has_holder = no }
				OR = {
					year = 590
					c_petuaria = { holder_scope = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no } }
				}
			}
		}
		independent = yes
		war = no
		year = 550
		OR = {
			NOT = { year = 590 }
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_landed_title = d_deira }
				NOT = { year = 620 }
			}
		}
		any_realm_province = {
			any_neighbor_province = {
				region = custom_deira
				ROOT_can_declare_war_against_province_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8
	}
		
	option = {
		name = "OK"
		random_province = {
			limit = {
				region = custom_deira
				ROOT_can_declare_war_against_province_trigger = yes
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { top_liege = { character = ROOT } }
				}
			}
			county = {
				declare_conquest_war = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					war = yes
				}
			}
			capital_scope = {
				ROOT = {
					spawn_unit = {
						province = PREV
						home = PREV
						owner = ROOT
						troops = {
							pikemen = { 350 350 }

						attrition = 0.5
						disband_on_peace = yes
					}
					if = {

							any_war = { defender = { num_of_count_titles_in_realm = 10 } }

# Saxon Invasions 490 AD, Venta and Portus Adurni (The Belgae)
narrative_event = {
	id = 313020
	title = "EVTNAME313020"
	desc = "EVTDESC313020"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_warships"
	
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		year = 490
		NOT = { year = 500 }
		war = no
		has_landed_title = k_sussex
		46 = {	# Portus Dubris
			owner = {
				realm = {								
					OR = { 
						title = e_aengland
						title = k_sussex
					}
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { completely_controls = c_venta }
			NOT = { completely_controls = c_portus_adurni }
			NOT = { completely_controls = c_vindomis }
		}
		NOR = {
			has_landed_title = d_the_belgae
			any_vassal = {
				has_landed_title = d_the_belgae
			}
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				6 = { # Venta
					owner = {
						top_liege = {
							is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
						}
					}
					ROOT_can_declare_war_against_province_trigger = yes
				}
				c_venta = {
					location = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							owner = {
								OR = {
									character = ROOT
									is_liege_or_above = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				15 = { # Portus Adurni
					owner = {
						top_liege = {
							is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
						}
					}
					ROOT_can_declare_war_against_province_trigger = yes
				}
				c_portus_adurni = {
					location = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							owner = {
								OR = {
									character = ROOT
									is_liege_or_above = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				361 = { # Vindomis
					owner = {
						top_liege = {
							is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
						}
					}
					ROOT_can_declare_war_against_province_trigger = yes
				}
				c_vindomis = {
					location = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							owner = {
								OR = {
									character = ROOT
									is_liege_or_above = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = sussex_invasion_490 }			
			had_global_flag = { flag = sussex_invasion_490 days = 1825 }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 493
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 495
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 500
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313020"
		trigger = {
			has_landed_title = k_sussex
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				6 = { # Venta
					owner = {
						top_liege = {
							is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
						}
					}
				}
				c_venta = {
					location = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							owner = {
								OR = {
									character = ROOT
									is_liege_or_above = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				set_character_flag = meonware_invader 
			}
			6 = {
				show_scope_change = no
				duchy = {
					show_scope_change = no
					ROOT = {
						show_scope_change = no
						unsafe_war = {
							casus_belli = duchy_invasion_event
							target = PREVPREV
							thirdparty_title = PREVPREV
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				361 = { # Vindomis
					owner = {
						top_liege = {
							is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
						}
					}
				}
				c_vindomis = {
					location = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							owner = {
								OR = {
									character = ROOT
									is_liege_or_above = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				set_character_flag = meonware_invader 
			}
			361 = {
				show_scope_change = no
				duchy = {
					show_scope_change = no
					ROOT = {
						show_scope_change = no
						unsafe_war = {
							casus_belli = duchy_invasion_event
							target = PREVPREV
							thirdparty_title = PREVPREV
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				15 = { # Portus Adurni
					owner = {
						top_liege = {
							is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
						}
					}
				}
				c_portus_adurni = {
					location = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							owner = {
								OR = {
									character = ROOT
									is_liege_or_above = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				set_character_flag = meonware_invader 
			}
			15 = {
				show_scope_change = no
				duchy = {
					show_scope_change = no
					ROOT = {
						show_scope_change = no
						unsafe_war = {
							casus_belli = duchy_invasion_event
							target = PREVPREV
							thirdparty_title = PREVPREV
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}		
		create_character = {
			random_traits = yes
			dynasty = random
			religion = germanic_pagan
			culture = oldsaxon
			female = no
			age = 33
			attributes = {
				martial = 12
			}
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
			trait = loyal
		}
		new_character = {
			spawn_unit = {
				province = 45 # Anderitum
				earmark = sussex_army_490
				troops = {
					light_infantry = { 1400 1400 }
					heavy_infantry = { 900 900 }
					pikemen = { 800 800 }
				}
				attrition = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = sussex_invasion_490 }		# Second time, give more troops
			spawn_unit = {
				province = 45 # Anderitum
				earmark = sussex_army_490
				troops = {
					light_infantry = { 500 500 }
					heavy_infantry = { 300 300 }
					pikemen = { 200 200 }
				}
				attrition = 1
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = sussex_invasion_490
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313020"
		trigger = {
			has_landed_title = k_sussex
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		prestige = -100
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC313020"	# Other Saxons
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
			NOT = { has_landed_title = k_sussex }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD313020"	# Britons
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture = briton
				culture = romanobritish
				culture = cumbrian
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTE313020"	# Others
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
			NOT = { culture = briton }
			NOT = { culture = romanobritish }
			NOT = { culture = cumbrian }
		}
	}
}
# Sussex grants Meonware to vassal
character_event = {
	id = 3130200
	desc = EVTDESC3130200
	picture = "GFX_evt_warships"
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_landed_title = k_sussex
		OR = {
			has_landed_title = c_venta
			has_landed_title = c_portus_adurni
			has_landed_title = c_vindomis
		}
		num_of_count_titles = 2
		completely_controls = d_the_belgae
		OR = {
			has_landed_title = d_the_belgae
			d_the_belgae = {
				has_holder = no
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_landed_title = d_hampshire }
		has_global_flag = meonware_conquered
		NOT = { has_global_flag = meonware_destroyed }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = meonware_granted }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}
	
	immediate = {
		create_character = {
			random_traits = yes
			name = "Port"
			dynasty = 818
			religion = germanic_pagan
			culture = jute
			female = no
			age = 25
		}
		new_character = {
			dynasty = 818
			wealth = 200
			save_event_target_as = port_of_meonware
		}
		set_global_flag = meonware_granted
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3130200	# Accept
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		event_target:port_of_meonware = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { 
						has_landed_title = c_venta
						num_of_count_titles = 2
					}
				}
				c_venta = { grant_title = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { 
						has_landed_title = c_portus_adurni
						num_of_count_titles = 2
					}
				}
				c_portus_adurni = { grant_title = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { 
						has_landed_title = c_vindomis
						num_of_count_titles = 2
					}
				}
				c_vindomis = { grant_title = PREV }
			}
			d_the_belgae = {
				grant_title = PREV 
			}
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3130200	# Refuse
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			event_target:port_of_meonware = {
				death = { death_reason = death_missing }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Change Culture and Religion upon Conquest
province_event = {
	id = 313023
	title = "EVTNAME313023"
	desc = "EVTDESC313023"
	
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_winter_village_crow"
	
	trigger = {
		d_west_saxons = {
			holder_scope = {
				capital_scope = {
					province = PREVPREVPREV
				}
			}
		}
		has_global_flag = west_saxon_invasion_534
		NOT = { has_province_flag = saxon_invasion }
		NOT = { has_province_flag = hamaland_saxon_invasion }
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = saxon_invasion_settlers }
			had_global_flag = { flag = saxon_invasion_settlers days = 1825 }
		}
		NOT = { culture = oldsaxon }
		owner = { culture = oldsaxon }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_province_flag = saxon_invasion
		set_global_flag = saxon_invasion_settlers
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313023"
		culture = oldsaxon
		religion = germanic_pagan
		if = {
			limit = { 
				any_province_holding = {
					is_capital = yes
					holding_type = castle
				}
			}
			germanic_convert_to_tribal_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = depopulated_1
			}
			remove_province_modifier = depopulated_1
			clr_province_flag = angeln_depopulation
			clr_province_flag = southern_britain_depopulation
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = depopulated_2
			}
			remove_province_modifier = depopulated_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = depopulated_3
			}
			remove_province_modifier = depopulated_3
		}
	}
}
# Maintain effort - Hampshire
character_event = {
	id = 313024
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	
	only_rulers = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = west_saxon_invasion_534
				OR = {
					has_landed_title = d_west_saxons
					AND = {
						has_character_flag = wessex_invader
						d_west_saxons = { has_holder = no }
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = west_saxon_invasion_534 }
				has_landed_title = k_wessex
				NOT = { num_of_count_titles_in_realm = 10 }
			}
		}
		independent = yes
		is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		war = no
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = west_saxon_invasion_hampshire
				OR = {
					NOT = { year = 560 }
					AND = {
						NOT = { year = 575 }
						has_global_flag = west_saxon_invasion_552
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = west_saxon_invasion_dorset
					has_global_flag = west_saxon_invasion_berkshire
				}
				year = 550
				OR = {
					NOT = { year = 575 }
					AND = {
						NOT = { year = 600 }
						has_global_flag = west_saxon_invasion_552
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = west_saxon_invasion_534 }
				year = 530
				NOT = { year = 560 }
			}
		}
		any_realm_province = {
			any_neighbor_province = {
				region = custom_hampshire
				ROOT_can_declare_war_against_province_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 6
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_global_flag = west_saxon_invasion_dorset
			NAND = {
				completely_controls = d_dorset
				has_global_flag = dorset_created
			}		
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			has_global_flag = west_saxon_invasion_berkshire
			NAND = {
				completely_controls = d_berkshire
				has_global_flag = berkshire_created
			}		
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
		# Try a non-Meonware province first
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = west_saxon_invasion_hampshire
					has_global_flag = west_saxon_invasion_dorset
				}
			}
			random_province = {
				limit = {
					region = custom_hampshire
					NOT = { region = custom_meonware }
					ROOT_can_declare_war_against_province_trigger = yes
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = { top_liege = { character = ROOT } }
					}
				}
				county = {
					declare_conquest_war = yes
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					war = no
				}
			}
			random_province = {
				limit = {
					region = custom_hampshire
					ROOT_can_declare_war_against_province_trigger = yes
					any_neighbor_province = {
						owner = { top_liege = { character = ROOT } }
					}
				}
				county = {
					declare_conquest_war = yes
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					war = yes
				}
			}
			capital_scope = {
				ROOT = {
					spawn_unit = {
						province = PREV
						home = PREV
						owner = ROOT
						troops = {
							light_infantry = { 300 300 }
							pikemen = { 450 450 }
							heavy_infantry = { 400 400 }
							archers = { 500 500 }
						}
						attrition = 0.5
					}
					spawn_unit = {
						province = PREV
						home = PREV
						owner = ROOT
						troops = {
							light_infantry = { 300 300 }
							pikemen = { 1200 1200 }
							heavy_infantry = { 800 800 }
							archers = { 500 500 }
						}
						disband_on_peace = yes
						attrition = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
			wealth = 70
		}
	}
}

# West Saxon Invasion 552 AD (2nd Try)
province_event = {
	id = 313025
	title = "EVTNAME313025"
	
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_warships"
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313025
		trigger = {		
			OR = {
				c_clausentum = {
					owner = {
						top_liege = {
							is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
						}
					}
				}
				c_vectis = {
					owner = {
						top_liege = {
							is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
						}
					}
				}
				c_portus_adurni = {
					owner = {
						top_liege = {
							is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
						}
					}
				}
				c_vindocladia = {
					owner = {
						top_liege = {
							is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
						}
					}
				}
				c_durnovaria = {
					owner = {
						top_liege = {
							is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313025_1
		trigger = {		
			c_clausentum = {
				owner = {
					top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes }
				}
			}
			c_vectis = {
				owner = {
					top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes }
				}
			}
			c_portus_adurni = {
				owner = {
					top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes }
				}
			}
			c_vindocladia = {
				owner = {
					top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes }
				}
			}
			c_durnovaria = {
				owner = {
					top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			province_id = 335	# Clausentum
			province_id = 10	# Vectis
			province_id = 15	# Portus Adurni
			province_id = 16	# Vindocladia
			province_id = 1		# Durnovaria
			AND = {
				OR = {
					province_id = 7		# Calleva
					province_id = 338	# Spinae
					province_id = 337	# Hen Vicus
				}
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = {
						top_liege = {
							is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { 
			holder_scope = 	{
				top_liege = { 
					is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
				}
			}
		}
		year = 550
		NOT = { year = 570 }
		has_global_flag = west_saxon_invasion_534
		NOT = { has_global_flag = west_saxon_invasion_552 }
		d_west_saxons = { has_holder = no }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = wessex_created }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 48
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 552
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 554
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 558
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		any_independent_ruler = {
			any_realm_province = {
				limit = { has_province_flag = west_saxon_invasion_province }
				clr_province_flag = west_saxon_invasion_province
			}
		}
		create_character = {
			random_traits = no
			name = "Cealwin"
			dynasty = 816
			religion = germanic_pagan
			culture = oldsaxon
			employer = d_west_saxons
			female = no
			age = 29
			attributes = {
				martial = 12
				diplomacy = 10
				stewardship = 12
				intrigue = 7
				learning = 8
			}
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = skilled_warrior
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
			trait = quick
			trait = light_foot_leader
			trait = ambitious
			trait = proud
			trait = wroth
		}
		new_character = {
			dynasty = 816
			set_character_flag = wessex_invader
			d_west_saxons = {
				activate_title = { title = d_west_saxons status = yes }
				gain_title = PREV
			}
			set_government_type = high_tribal_government
			character_event = { id = 313022 }
			character_event = { id = 313026 }
			wealth = 100
			prestige = 500
			create_character = {
				name="Æscwine"
				random_traits = yes
				dynasty = random
				religion = germanic_pagan
				culture = oldsaxon
				female = no
				employer = d_west_saxons
				age = 31
				attributes = {
					martial = 15
					stewardship = 10
					diplomacy = 12
				}
				trait = brilliant_strategist
				trait = war_hero
				trait = brave
				trait = loyal
				trait = heavy_infantry_leader
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = west_saxon_invasion_552
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313025"	# Other Saxons
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313025"	# Britons
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture = briton
				culture = romanobritish
				culture = cumbrian
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC313025"	# Others
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
			NOT = { culture = briton }
			NOT = { culture = romanobritish }
			NOT = { culture = cumbrian }
		}
	}
}

# Kill off Caraticos so that Cynric inherits Wiht (or if he lives for too long)
character_event = {
	id = 313028
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	only_men = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
			}
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						location = { region = world_britannia }
						capital_scope = { region = world_britannia }
					}
				}
				ROOT = { 
					if = {
						limit = { independent = no }
						liege = {
							grant_title_no_opinion = PREVPREV
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							job_chancellor = {
								is_ruler = no
								NOR = { 
									dynasty = ROOT
									is_close_relative = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
						job_chancellor = {
							save_event_target_as = new_ruler
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							job_marshal = {
								is_ruler = no
								NOR = { 
									dynasty = ROOT
									is_close_relative = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
						job_marshal = {
							save_event_target_as = new_ruler
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							any_courtier = {
								is_adult = yes
								is_female = no
								is_ruler = no
								culture = ROOT
								religion = ROOT
								NOR = { 
									dynasty = ROOT
									is_close_relative = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
						random_courtier = {
							limit = {
								is_adult = yes
								is_female = no
								is_ruler = no
								culture = ROOT
								religion = ROOT
								NOR = { 
									dynasty = ROOT
									is_close_relative = ROOT
								}
							}
							save_event_target_as = new_ruler
						}
					}
					else = {
						create_character = {
							random_traits = yes
							dynasty = culture
							religion = ROOT
							culture = ROOT
							female = no
							employer = ROOT
							random_traits = yes
							age = 24
						}
						new_character = {
							save_event_target_as = new_ruler
						}
					}
					event_target:new_ruler = {
						grant_title_no_opinion = PREVPREV
						if = {
							limit = { ROOT = { independent = no } }
							ROOT = { liege = { set_defacto_vassal = PREVPREV } }
						}
						else = {
							set_defacto_liege = THIS
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		death = { 
			death_reason = death_natural
		}
	}
}

# East Anglian Invasions 450 AD, settlers land on Nortwic (1st Invasion)
province_event = {
	id = 313300
	title = "EVTNAME313300"
	desc = "EVTDESC313300"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_anglosaxons_ashore"
	
	trigger = {
		province_id = 153	# Nortwic
		year = 450
		NOT = { year = 475 }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = anglian_east_invasion_450 }
		owner = {
			top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.05
			c_nortwic = {
				holder_scope = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							independent = yes
							lower_tier_than = KING
						}
						top_liege = {
							lower_tier_than = KING
						}
						war = yes
					}
				}
			}					
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 465
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 467
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 469
		}
	}
		
	immediate = {
		create_character = {
			random_traits = no
			name = "Tyttman"
			dynasty = 826
			religion = germanic_pagan
			culture = angle
			employer = d_angles
			female = no
			age = 31
			attributes = {
				martial = 15
				diplomacy = 14
				stewardship = 13
				intrigue = 11
				learning = 10
			}
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = skilled_warrior
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
			trait = quick
			trait = heavy_infantry_leader
			#trait = authoritative
			trait = lustful
			trait = just
		}
		new_character = {
			dynasty = 826
			set_character_flag = anglia_invader
			d_angles = {
				activate_title = { title = d_angles status = yes }
				gain_title = PREV
			}
			set_government_type = high_tribal_government
			d_norfolc = {
				add_claim = PREV
			}
			c_nortwic = {
				add_claim = PREV
			}
			c_elmham = {
				add_claim = PREV
			}
			c_thetford = {
				add_claim = PREV
			}
			c_swaffham = {
				add_claim = PREV
			}
			character_event = { id = 313301 }
			wealth = 200
			prestige = 500
			create_character = {
				name="Eoric"
				random_traits = yes
				dynasty = 826
				religion = germanic_pagan
				culture = angle
				female = no
				employer = d_angles
				age = 36
				attributes = {
					martial = 13
					stewardship = 10
					diplomacy = 12
				}
				trait = brilliant_strategist
				trait = war_hero
				trait = brave
				trait = loyal
				trait = heavy_infantry_leader
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = anglian_east_invasion_450
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313300"	# Other Saxons
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313300"	# Britons
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture = briton
				culture = romanobritish
				culture = cumbrian
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC313300"	# Others
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
			NOT = { culture = briton }
			NOT = { culture = romanobritish }
			NOT = { culture = cumbrian }
		}
	}
	
}

		province_id = 153	# Nortwic
		has_global_flag = anglian_east_invasion_450
		NOT = { has_province_flag = anglian_invasion }
		NOT = { culture = angle }
		owner = { culture = angle }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_province_flag = anglian_invasion
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313302"
		culture = angle
		religion = germanic_pagan
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = depopulated_1
			}
			remove_province_modifier = depopulated_1
			clr_province_flag = angeln_depopulation
			clr_province_flag = southern_britain_depopulation
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = depopulated_2
			}
			remove_province_modifier = depopulated_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = depopulated_3
			}
			remove_province_modifier = depopulated_3
		}
	}
}

			has_earmarked_regiments = east_angles_army_469

# East Angles create Jarldom of Norfolc
character_event = {
	id = 313308
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_men = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		age = 20
		has_landed_title = d_angles
		has_landed_title = c_nortwic
		num_of_count_titles = 2
		NOT = { has_landed_title = d_norfolc }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = norfolc_created }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 6
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
		d_norfolc = { gain_title = ROOT }
		disband_event_forces = east_angles_army_450
		disband_event_forces = east_angles_army_469
	}
}

# Iclingas Invasion 570 AD
province_event = {
	id = 313050
	title = "EVTNAME313050"
	desc = "EVTDESC313050"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_saxon_army"
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			region = custom_pegansaete
			region = custom_tomsaete
			region = custom_middleanglia
			region = custom_grentbryce
		}
		any_neighbor_province = {
			OR = {
				owner = {
					top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes }
				}
				province_id = 312	# Metaris Æstuarium
			}
		}
		year = 570
		NOT = { year = 590 }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_560	}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = mercia_created }
		NOT = { 
			owner = {
				top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes }
			}
		}
		k_mercia = { has_holder = no }
		d_iclingas = { has_holder = no }
		NOR = {
			event_target:mercia_claimant = {
				always = yes
			}
			event_target:mercia_invader = {
				is_alive = yes
				is_ruler = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 48
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 572
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			year = 574
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			year = 576
		}
	}
		
	immediate = {
		create_character = {
			random_traits = no
			name = "Cynewald"
			dynasty = 819
			religion = germanic_pagan
			culture = angle
			employer = d_north_angles
			female = no
			age = 30
			attributes = {
				martial = 12
				diplomacy = 12
				stewardship = 9
				intrigue = 12
				learning = 8
			}
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = skilled_warrior
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
			trait = quick
			trait = light_foot_leader
			trait = wroth
			trait = lustful
			trait = charitable
		}
		new_character = {
			dynasty = 819
			set_character_flag = cynewald_of_mercia
			set_character_flag = mercia_invader
			save_global_event_target_as = cynewald_of_mercia
			save_global_event_target_as = mercia_invader
			d_iclingas = {
				activate_title = { title = d_iclingas status = yes }
				gain_title = PREV
				succession = elective_gavelkind
			}
			set_government_type = high_tribal_government
			character_event = { id = 313051 }
			#character_event = { id = 3130571 }
			wealth = 100
			prestige = 500
			create_character = {
				name="Eorweald"
				random_traits = yes
				dynasty = random
				religion = germanic_pagan
				culture = angle
				female = no
				employer = d_iclingas
				age = 25
				attributes = {
					martial = 13
					stewardship = 10
					diplomacy = 12
				}
				trait = brilliant_strategist
				trait = war_hero
				trait = brave
				trait = loyal
				trait = heavy_infantry_leader
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_560
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313050"	# Other Saxons
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313050"	# Britons
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture = briton
				culture = romanobritish
				culture = cumbrian
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC313050"	# Others
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
			NOT = { culture = briton }
			NOT = { culture = romanobritish }
			NOT = { culture = cumbrian }
		}
	}
}
