# Change Culture and Religion upon Conquest
province_event = {
	id = 313055
	title = "EVTNAME313055"
	desc = "EVTDESC313055"
	
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_winter_village_crow"
	
	trigger = {
		d_iclingas = {
			holder_scope = {
				capital_scope = {
					province = PREVPREVPREV
				}
			}
		}
		has_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_560
		NOT = { has_province_flag = mercia_anglian_invasion }
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = mercia_anglian_invasion_settlers }
			had_global_flag = { flag = mercia_anglian_invasion_settlers days = 1825 }
		}
		NOT = { culture = angle }
		owner = { culture = angle }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_province_flag = mercia_anglian_invasion
		set_global_flag = mercia_anglian_invasion_settlers
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313055"
		culture = angle
		religion = germanic_pagan
		if = {
			limit = { 
				any_province_holding = {
					is_capital = yes
					holding_type = castle
				}
			}
			germanic_convert_to_tribal_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = depopulated_1
			}
			remove_province_modifier = depopulated_1
			clr_province_flag = angeln_depopulation
			clr_province_flag = southern_britain_depopulation
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = depopulated_2
			}
			remove_province_modifier = depopulated_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = depopulated_3
			}
			remove_province_modifier = depopulated_3
		}
	}
}
# Maintain effort - Middle Anglia
character_event = {
	id = 313056
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	
	only_rulers = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		#has_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_560
		has_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_middle_anglia
		OR = {
			has_landed_title = d_iclingas
			AND = {
				has_character_flag = mercia_invader
				d_iclingas = { has_holder = no }
			}
			AND = {
				has_claim = k_mercia
				event_target:mercia_claimant = {
					character = ROOT
				}
				NOT = { has_global_flag = mercia_created }
			}
		}
		independent = yes
		is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		war = no
		OR = {
			NOT = { year = 595 }
			AND = {
				NOT = { year = 615 }
				has_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_580
			}
		}
		any_realm_province = {
			any_neighbor_province = {
				region = custom_middleanglia
				ROOT_can_declare_war_against_province_trigger = yes
			}
		}			
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 6
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			realm_size = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			realm_size = 6
		}
	}
		
	option = {
		name = "OK"
		random_province = {
			limit = {
				region = custom_middleanglia
				ROOT_can_declare_war_against_province_trigger = yes
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { top_liege = { character = ROOT } }
				}
			}
			county = {
				declare_conquest_war = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { war = yes	}
			capital_scope = {
				ROOT = {
					spawn_unit = {
						province = PREV
						home = PREV
						owner = ROOT
						troops = {
							light_infantry = { 400 400 }
							pikemen = { 250 250 }
							heavy_infantry = { 200 200 }
							archers = { 200 200 }
						}
						attrition = 0.5
					}
					spawn_unit = {
						province = PREV
						home = PREV
						owner = ROOT
						troops = {
							light_infantry = { 700 700 }
							pikemen = { 450 450 }
							heavy_infantry = { 600 600 }
							archers = { 400 400 }
						}
						disband_on_peace = yes
						attrition = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
			wealth = 70
		}
	}
}

							light_infantry = { 700 700 }
							pikemen = { 450 450 }
							heavy_infantry = { 600 600 }
							archers = { 400 400 }
						}

				}

		}
	}

# Iclingas Invasion 590 AD (2nd Try)
province_event = {
	id = 313057
	title = "EVTNAME313057"
	desc = EVTDESC313057
	
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_saxon_army"	
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			region = custom_pegansaete
			region = custom_tomsaete
			region = custom_middleanglia
			region = custom_grentbryce
		}
		any_neighbor_province = {
			OR = {
				owner = {
					top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes }
				}
				province_id = 312	# Metaris Æstuarium
			}
		}
		NOT = { 
			holder_scope = 	{
				top_liege = { 
					is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
				}
			}
		}
		year = 590
		NOT = { year = 620 }
		#has_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_560
		NOT = { has_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_580 }
		k_mercia = { has_holder = no }
		d_iclingas = { has_holder = no }
		NOR = {
			event_target:mercia_claimant = {
				always = yes
			}
			event_target:mercia_invader = {
				is_alive = yes
				is_ruler = yes
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = mercia_created }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 48
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 582
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 584
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 586
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		any_independent_ruler = {
			any_realm_province = {
				limit = { has_province_flag = iclingas_invasion_province }
				clr_province_flag = iclingas_invasion_province
			}
		}
		create_character = {
			random_traits = no
			name = "Creoda"
			dynasty = 819
			religion = germanic_pagan
			culture = angle
			employer = d_iclingas
			female = no
			age = 28
			attributes = {
				martial = 12
				diplomacy = 10
				stewardship = 12
				intrigue = 7
				learning = 8
			}
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = skilled_warrior
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
			trait = quick
			trait = heavy_infantry_leader
			trait = ambitious
			trait = patient
			trait = envious
		}
		new_character = {
			dynasty = 819
			set_character_flag = mercia_invader
			save_global_event_target_as = mercia_invader
			d_iclingas = {
				activate_title = { title = d_iclingas status = yes }
				gain_title = PREV
			}
			set_government_type = high_tribal_government
			character_event = { id = 313051 }
			character_event = { id = 3130570 }
			wealth = 150
			prestige = 500
			create_character = {
				name="thelræd"
				random_traits = yes
				dynasty = random
				religion = germanic_pagan
				culture = angle
				female = no
				employer = d_iclingas
				age = 37
				attributes = {
					martial = 15
					stewardship = 10
					diplomacy = 12
				}
				trait = brilliant_strategist
				trait = war_hero
				trait = brave
				trait = loyal
				trait = heavy_infantry_leader
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_580
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313057"	# Other Saxons
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313057"	# Britons
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture = briton
				culture = romanobritish
				culture = cumbrian
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC313057"	# Others
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
			NOT = { culture = briton }
			NOT = { culture = romanobritish }
			NOT = { culture = cumbrian }
		}
	}
}

### ALTERNATE RISE OF THE ICLINGAS - FROM SETTLEMENT (CLAIM ICLINGAS DECISION) ###
# Revolt for independence
character_event = {
	id = 313070
	title = "EVTNAME313070"
	desc = "EVTDESC313070"
	picture = "GFX_evt_saxon_army"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = claiming_iclingas
	}		
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA313070
		save_global_event_target_as = iclingas_revolter
		if = {
			limit = { trait = loyal }
			remove_trait = loyal
		}
		capital_scope = {
			ROOT = {
				spawn_unit = {
					owner = ROOT
					province = PREV
					home = ROOT
					troops = {
						archers = { 350 350 }
						light_infantry = { 500 500 }
						heavy_infantry = { 450 450 }
					}
					attrition = 0.5
					maintenance_multiplier = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ai = yes }
			capital_scope = {
				ROOT = {
					spawn_unit = {
						owner = ROOT
						province = PREV
						troops = {
							archers = { 350 350 }
							light_infantry = { 600 600 }
							heavy_infantry = { 350 350 }
						}
						attrition = 0.5
						maintenance_multiplier = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						independent = no
						liege = { 
							realm_size = 10 
						} 
					}
					AND = {
						is_tributary = yes
						suzerain = { 
							realm_size = 10 
						} 
					}
				}
			}
			capital_scope = {
				ROOT = {
					spawn_unit = {
						owner = ROOT
						province = PREV
						troops = {
							archers = { 250 250 }
							light_infantry = { 450 450 }
							heavy_infantry = { 350 350 }
						}
						attrition = 0.5
						disband_on_peace = yes
						maintenance_multiplier = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						independent = no
						liege = { 
							realm_size = 20 
						} 
					}
					AND = {
						is_tributary = yes
						suzerain = { 
							realm_size = 20 
						} 
					}
				}
			}
			capital_scope = {
				ROOT = {
					spawn_unit = {
						owner = ROOT
						province = PREV
						troops = {
							archers = { 300 300 }
							light_infantry = { 350 350 }
							heavy_infantry = { 350 350 }
						}
						attrition = 0.5
						maintenance_multiplier = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						independent = no
						liege = { 
							realm_size = 30 
						} 
					}
					AND = {
						is_tributary = yes
						suzerain = { 
							realm_size = 30 
						} 
					}
				}
			}
			capital_scope = {
				ROOT = {
					spawn_unit = {
						owner = ROOT
						province = PREV
						troops = {
							archers = { 200 200 }
							light_infantry = { 300 300 }
							heavy_infantry = { 75 75 }
						}
						attrition = 0.5
						disband_on_peace = yes
						maintenance_multiplier = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { independent = no }
			liege = {
				ROOT = {
					war = {
						target = PREV
						casus_belli = bid_for_independence
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			suzerain = {
				ROOT = {
					war = {
						target = PREV
						casus_belli = free_tributary_cb
					}
				}
			}			
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = claimed_iclingas_timer
				duration = 1825
			}
		}
	}
}

narrative_event = {
	id = 313071

						tier = COUNT
						region = custom_middleanglia
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_middle_anglia
			break = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					any_demesne_title = {
						tier = COUNT

					}

				dynasty = 819

					dynasty = 819
					any_child = {
						dynasty = 819
					}
				}
			}
		}
		father_even_if_dead = {
			any_child = {
				limit = {
					is_ruler = no

				}
				dynasty = 819
				any_child = {
					limit = { is_ruler = no }
					dynasty = 819
					any_child = {
						limit = { is_ruler = no }
						dynasty = 819
					}

			new_character = {

				}

			if = {

				}

					}
					AND = {

						has_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_tomsaete
					}

						has_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_pegansaete

					}

						region = custom_cilternsaete
						has_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_cilternsaete
					}
					AND = {
						region = custom_hwicce
						has_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_hwicce
					}
				}

			}

			county = {
				add_claim = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { ai = yes } }

				limit = {
					has_province_flag = iclingas_target_county

					}
				}
				county = {
					declare_conquest_war = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB313071
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = claiming_iclingas }
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
			capital_scope = {
				region = custom_mercia
			}

	}

		name = EVTOPTC313071
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = claiming_iclingas }
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					capital_scope = {
						region = custom_mercia
					}
				}

					character = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD313071
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = claiming_iclingas }
			is_brythonic_culture_trigger = yes
		}

				is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
				is_brythonic_culture_trigger = yes

					}

			}

					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {

			capital_scope = {
				ROOT = {
					spawn_unit = {

						}

						disband_on_peace = yes
						maintenance_multiplier = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
		}
		liege = {

					target = PREV
					casus_belli = bid_for_independence
				}
			}
		}
	}

						troops = {
								archers = { 200 200 }
								light_infantry = { 150 150 }

				}
				create_character = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = random
					religion = ROOT
					culture = ROOT
					female = no
					age = 35
					attributes = {
						martial = 11

					}
				}
			}
		}

# Cleanup event
character_event = {
	id = 313078
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	picture = "GFX_evt_saxon_army_banners"
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_claim = k_mercia
			has_character_flag = claiming_mercia
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = mercia_created }
		OR = {
			is_ruler = no
			NOT = {
				event_target:mercia_claimant = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:mercia_claimant = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			clear_global_event_target = mercia_claimant
			clr_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_middle_anglia
			clr_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_tomsaete
			clr_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_pegansaete
			clr_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_grentbryce
			clr_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_wrocensaete
			clr_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_magonsaete
			clr_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_cilternsaete
			clr_global_flag = iclingas_invasion_hwicce
			any_province = {
				clr_province_flag = iclingas_target_county
			}
		}
		remove_claim = k_mercia
		clr_character_flag = claiming_mercia
	}
}

	picture = "GFX_evt_saxon_army_banners"
	
	hide_window = yes

		has_claim = k_mercia
		event_target:mercia_claimant = {
			character = ROOT
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = mercia_created }
	}
	
	immediate = {

		current_heir = {
			save_global_event_target_as = mercia_claimant
			add_pressed_claim = k_mercia
			set_character_flag = claiming_mercia
		}
	}

# Hwiccas Invasion 577 AD
province_event = {
	id = 313060
	title = "EVTNAME313060"
	desc = "EVTDESC313060"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_saxon_army_banners"
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			region = custom_hwicce
			province_id = 340	# Ariconium
			province_id = 23	# Lactodorum
			region = custom_cilternsaete
		}
		any_neighbor_province = {
			owner = {
				top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes }
			}
		}
		year = 577
		NOT = { year = 610 }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = hwicce_invasion_577 }
		d_hwicce = { has_holder = no }
		owner = {
			top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no }
		}
		NOT = {
			event_target:hwicce_invader = {
				is_alive = yes
				is_landed = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 48
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 580
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			year = 582
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			year = 584
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		create_character = {
			random_traits = no
			name = "Eanhere"
			dynasty = 820
			religion = germanic_pagan
			culture = oldsaxon
			employer = d_hwiccas
			female = no
			age = 32
			attributes = {
				martial = 9
				diplomacy = 8
				stewardship = 6
				intrigue = 7
				learning = 6
			}
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = skilled_warrior
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
			trait = quick
			trait = light_foot_leader
			trait = cruel
			trait = trusting
			trait = patient
		}
		new_character = {
			dynasty = 820
			set_character_flag = eanhere_of_hwicce
			set_character_flag = hwicce_invader
			save_global_event_target_as = hwicce_invader
			d_hwiccas = {
				activate_title = { title = d_hwiccas status = yes }
				gain_title = PREV
				succession = elective_gavelkind
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { government = high_tribal_government } }
				set_government_type = high_tribal_government
			}
			character_event = { id = 313061 }
			wealth = 300
			prestige = 500
			create_character = {
				name="Æthelric"
				random_traits = yes
				dynasty = random
				religion = germanic_pagan
				culture = oldsaxon
				female = no
				employer = d_hwiccas
				age = 28
				attributes = {
					martial = 9
					stewardship = 6
					diplomacy = 7
				}
				trait = brilliant_strategist
				trait = war_hero
				trait = brave
				trait = loyal
				trait = heavy_infantry_leader
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = hwicce_invasion_577
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313060"	# Other Saxons
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313060"	# Britons
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture = briton
				culture = romanobritish
				culture = cumbrian
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC313060"	# Others
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
			NOT = { culture = briton }
			NOT = { culture = romanobritish }
			NOT = { culture = cumbrian }
		}
	}
}

					}
				}
				location = { set_province_flag = hwiccas_invasion_province }
			}
			set_global_flag = hwiccas_invasion_hwicce
			character_event = { id = 313063 }	# Spawn Troops
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				war = no
				c_tripontium = {
					owner = {
						top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no }
					}
					location = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							owner = {
								top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = { 
				add_claim = c_glevum 
				add_claim = c_aquae_sulis
				add_claim = c_corinium
				add_claim = c_avona
				add_claim = c_tripontium
			}
			c_tripontium = { 
				owner = {
					top_liege = {
						c_tripontium = { 
							reverse_war = {
								target = d_hwiccas
								casus_belli = claim
							}
						}
					}
				}
				location = { set_province_flag = hwiccas_invasion_province }
			}
			set_global_flag = hwiccas_invasion_hwicce
			character_event = { id = 313063 }	# Spawn Troops
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				war = no
				c_ariconium = {
					owner = {
						top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no }
					}
					location = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							owner = {
								top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = { 
				add_claim = c_glevum 
				add_claim = c_aquae_sulis
				add_claim = c_corinium
				add_claim = c_avona
				add_claim = c_ariconium
			}
			c_ariconium = { 
				owner = {
					top_liege = {
						c_ariconium = { 
							reverse_war = {
								target = d_hwiccas
								casus_belli = claim
							}
						}
					}
				}
				location = { set_province_flag = hwiccas_invasion_province }
			}
			set_global_flag = hwiccas_invasion_hwicce
			character_event = { id = 313063 }	# Spawn Troops
		}
		if = {
			limit = { war = no }
			character_event = { id = 313062 }	# Move on to Cilternsaete
		}
	}
}

# Change Culture and Religion upon Conquest
province_event = {
	id = 313064
	title = "EVTNAME313064"
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313064
		trigger = {
			religion_group = christian
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313064_1
		trigger = {
			NOT = { religion_group = christian }
		}
	}
	
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_winter_village_crow"
	
	trigger = {
		d_hwiccas = {
			holder_scope = {
				capital_scope = {
					province = PREVPREVPREV
				}
			}
		}
		has_global_flag = hwicce_invasion_577
		NOT = { has_province_flag = hwicce_anglian_invasion }
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = hwicce_anglian_invasion_settlers }
			had_global_flag = { flag = hwicce_anglian_invasion_settlers days = 1825 }
		}
		NOT = { culture = oldsaxon }
		owner = { culture = oldsaxon }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_province_flag = hwicce_anglian_invasion
		set_global_flag = hwicce_anglian_invasion_settlers
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313064"
		culture = oldsaxon
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { religion_group = christian } }
			religion = germanic_pagan
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = depopulated_1
			}
			remove_province_modifier = depopulated_1
			clr_province_flag = angeln_depopulation
			clr_province_flag = southern_britain_depopulation
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = depopulated_2
			}
			remove_province_modifier = depopulated_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = depopulated_3
			}
			remove_province_modifier = depopulated_3
		}
	}
}
# Maintain effort - Hwicce
character_event = {
	id = 313065
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	
	only_rulers = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		has_global_flag = hwicce_invasion_577
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = hwiccas_invasion_hwicce
			has_global_flag = hwiccas_invasion_cilternsaete
		}
		OR = {
			has_landed_title = d_hwiccas
			has_landed_title = d_hwicce
			AND = {
				has_character_flag = hwicce_invader
				d_hwiccas = { has_holder = no }
			}
		}
		dynasty = 820
		independent = yes
		is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		war = no
		OR = {
			NOT = { year = 600 }
			AND = {
				NOT = { year = 625 }
				has_global_flag = hwicce_invasion_595
			}
		}
		any_realm_province = {
			any_neighbor_province = {
				region = custom_hwicce
				ROOT_can_declare_war_against_province_trigger = yes
			}
		}			
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 6
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			realm_size = 4
			has_global_flag = hwiccas_invasion_hwicce
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			realm_size = 6
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 6
			has_global_flag = hwiccas_invasion_cilternsaete
			NOT = { has_global_flag = cilternsaete_created }
			NOT = { completely_controls = d_cilternsaete }
		}			
	}
		
	option = {
		name = "OK"
		random_province = {
			limit = {
				region = custom_hwicce
				ROOT_can_declare_war_against_province_trigger = yes
				any_neighbor_province = {
					owner = { top_liege = { character = ROOT } }
				}
			}
			county = {
				declare_conquest_war = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { war = yes	}
			capital_scope = {
				ROOT = {
					spawn_unit = {
						province = PREV
						home = PREV
						owner = ROOT
						troops = {
							light_infantry = { 400 400 }
							pikemen = { 300 300 }
							heavy_infantry = { 250 250 }
							archers = { 250 250 }
						}
						attrition = 0.5
					}
					spawn_unit = {
						province = PREV
						home = PREV
						owner = ROOT
						troops = {
							light_infantry = { 800 800 }
							pikemen = { 600 600 }
							heavy_infantry = { 550 550 }
							archers = { 500 500 }
						}
						disband_on_peace = yes
						attrition = 0.5
					}
					wealth = 100
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Hwiccas Invasion 595 AD (2nd Try)
province_event = {
	id = 313067
	title = "EVTNAME313067"
	desc = EVTDESC313067
	
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_saxon_army"	
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			region = custom_hwicce
			province_id = 340	# Ariconium
			province_id = 23	# Lactodorum
			region = custom_cilternsaete
		}
		any_neighbor_province = {
			owner = {
				top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes }
			}
		}
		year = 595
		NOT = { year = 620 }
		has_global_flag = hwicce_invasion_577
		NOT = { has_global_flag = hwicce_invasion_595 }
		d_hwiccas = { has_holder = no }
		d_hwicce = { has_holder = no }
		NOT = { 
			owner = {
				top_liege = { is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes }
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			event_target:hwicce_invader = {
				is_alive = yes
				is_landed = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 48
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 597
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 599
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 601
		}
	}
	

	immediate = {
		any_independent_ruler = {
			any_realm_province = {
				limit = { has_province_flag = hwiccas_invasion_province }
				clr_province_flag = hwiccas_invasion_province
			}
		}
		create_character = {
			random_traits = no
			name = "Eanfrith"
			dynasty = 820
			religion = germanic_pagan
			culture = oldsaxon
			employer = d_hwiccas
			female = no
			age = 27
			attributes = {
				martial = 9
				diplomacy = 8
				stewardship = 6
				intrigue = 5
				learning = 7
			}
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = skilled_warrior
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
			trait = quick
			trait = heavy_infantry_leader
			trait = cruel
			trait = diligent
		}
		new_character = {
			dynasty = 820
			set_character_flag = hwicce_invader
			save_global_event_target_as = hwicce_invader
			d_hwiccas = {
				activate_title = { title = d_hwiccas status = yes }
				gain_title = PREV
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { government = high_tribal_government } }
				set_government_type = high_tribal_government
			}
			character_event = { id = 313068 }
			character_event = { id = 313061 }
			wealth = 1500
			prestige = 500
			create_character = {
				name="Cuthræd"
				random_traits = yes
				dynasty = random
				religion = germanic_pagan
				culture = oldsaxon
				female = no
				employer = d_hwiccas
				age = 34
				attributes = {
					martial = 9
					stewardship = 8
					diplomacy = 10
				}
				trait = brilliant_strategist
				trait = war_hero
				trait = brave
				trait = loyal
				trait = heavy_infantry_leader
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = hwicce_invasion_595
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313067"	# Other Saxons
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313067"	# Britons
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture = briton
				culture = romanobritish
				culture = cumbrian
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC313067"	# Others
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
			NOT = { culture = briton }
			NOT = { culture = romanobritish }
			NOT = { culture = cumbrian }
		}
	}
}

# Set right father
character_event = {
	id = 313068
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		any_independent_ruler = {
			any_realm_character = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = eanhere_of_hwicce }
				ROOT = {
					set_father = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
	}
}

# Conversion of Hwicce
character_event = {
	id = 313069
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	
	only_rulers = yes
	ai = yes
	
	trigger = {
		year = 590
		OR = {
			has_landed_title = d_hwiccas
			has_landed_title = d_hwicce
			has_character_flag = hwicce_invader
		}
		NOT = { religion_group = christian }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 120
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			capital_scope = {
				religion = catholic
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			capital_scope = {
				religion_group = christian
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_spouse = {
				religion_group = christian
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 600
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 605
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 610
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 615
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 620
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		religion = catholic
		any_child = {
			religion = catholic
		}
		any_vassal = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = zealous } }
			religion = catholic
		}
		capital_scope = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { religion_group = christian } }
				religion = catholic
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
	}
}

### RISE OF LINDSEY ###

# Angles of Linnius give ultimatum
character_event = {
	id = 313030
	title = "EVTNAME313030"
	desc = "EVTDESC313030"
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_warships"
	
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_character_flag = angle_sending_ultimatum
			AND = {
				ai = yes		# Human player triggers by decision
				year = 470
				NOT = { year = 510 }
				war = no
				is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
				has_landed_title = c_ad_abum
				c_ad_abum = {
					location = {
						is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
						has_province_modifier = anglosaxon_settlement
					}
				}
				tier = count
				trait = foederate
				OR = {
					AND = {
						independent = no
						liege = {
							culture_group = celtic
						}
					}
					AND = {
						is_tributary = { type = foederati }
						suzerain = {
							culture_group = celtic
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = angles_lindsey_ultimatum }
					had_global_flag =  { flag = angles_lindsey_ultimatum days = 3650 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 180
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			year = 475
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 480
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			year = 485
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = angle_sending_ultimatum
		set_global_flag = angles_lindsey_ultimatum
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313030"	# Send Ultimatum
		ai_chance = { factor = 95 }
		if = {
			limit = { independent = no }
			liege = {
				character_event = {	id = 313031 days = 1 }
			}
			break = yes
		}
		suzerain = {
			character_event = {	id = 313031 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313030"	# Don't send ultimatum
		trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 5 
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOR = {
					trait = loyal
					trait = content
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					trait = unloyal
					trait = ambitious 
				}
			}
		}
		prestige = -100
	}
}

# Liege receives ultimatum
character_event = {
	id = 313031
	title = "EVTNAME313031"
	desc = "EVTDESC313031"
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_emissary"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { independent = no }
			liege = { save_event_target_as = linnius_liege }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313031"	# Accept Ultimatum
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 80 
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				top_liege = {
					realm_size = 2
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				top_liege = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				top_liege = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				top_liege = {
					realm_size = 20
				}
			}
		}
		prestige = -200
		FROM = {
			character_event = {	id = 313032 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313031"	# Refuse ultimatum
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		prestige = 100
		if = {
			limit = { independent = no }
			liege = { save_event_target_as = linnius_liege }
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {	id = 313034 days = 1 }
		}
		set_character_flag = lindsey_proper_liege
	}
}

# Ultimatum Accepted
narrative_event = {
	id = 313032
	title = "EVTNAME313032"
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_saxon_army_banners"
	
	major = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# Victorious Angles
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313032
		trigger = {
			character = ROOT
		}
	}
	
	# Former ruler of Linnius
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313032_1
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
	}
	
	# Linnius liege, if there is one
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313032_2
		trigger = {
			event_target:linnius_liege = {
				character = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Other Anglo-Saxons
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313032_3
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				character = ROOT
				character = FROM
				event_target:linnius_liege = {
					character = PREV
				}
			}
			culture_group = germanic
			is_romanized_germanic_trigger = no
		}
	}
	
	# Other Britons
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313032_4
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				character = ROOT
				character = FROM
				event_target:linnius_liege = {
					character = PREV
				}
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { culture_group = germanic }
				is_romanized_germanic_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	major_trigger = {
		OR = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
			is_brythonic_culture_trigger = yes
			capital_scope = {
				region = world_britannia
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { independent = yes }
			suzerain = {
				save_event_target_as = former_liege
			}
			break = yes
		}
		liege = {
			save_event_target_as = former_liege
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313032"
		trigger = {
			character = ROOT
		}
		prestige = 200
		event_target:former_liege = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_landed_title = d_lindum
					num_of_duke_titles = 1
					tier = duke
				}
				any_vassal = {
					limit = { tier = count }
					set_character_flag = lindsey_vassal
				}
				set_character_flag = lindsey_vassal
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						num_of_duke_titles = 2
						tier = king
						NOT = { has_landed_title = d_lindum }
					}
				}
				c_banovallum = {
					holder_scope = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								num_of_count_titles = 1
								tier = count
								same_realm = FROM
							}
							set_character_flag = lindsey_vassal
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									OR = {
										num_of_count_titles = 1
										tier = count
									}
								}
								same_realm = FROM
							}
							PREV = { grant_title = ROOT }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_lindum = {
					holder_scope = {
						same_realm = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			c_lindum = {
				grant_title = ROOT
				hidden_tooltip = {
					location = {
						province_event = {
							id = 55002
							days = 365
							random = 100
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		d_lindsey = { grant_title = ROOT }
		d_lindum = { destroy_landed_title = d_lindum }
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = lindsey_vassal }
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
			clr_character_flag = lindsey_vassal
		}
		set_defacto_liege = THIS
		138 = {
			remove_province_modifier = anglosaxon_settlement
		}
		create_character = {
			random_traits = yes
			dynasty = random
			religion = germanic_pagan
			culture = angle
			female = no
			age = 30
			attributes = {
				martial = 10
			}
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
			trait = skilled_warrior
		}
		new_character = {
			spawn_unit = {
				province = 138 # Caistor
				troops =
				{
					light_infantry = { 700 700 }
					heavy_infantry = { 550 550 }
					pikemen = { 400 400 }
					archers = { 300 300 }
				}
				attrition = 0.5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		name = "EVTOPTB313032"
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:linnius_liege = {
				character = PREV
			}
		}
		name = "EVTOPTC313032"
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				character = ROOT
				character = FROM
				event_target:linnius_liege = {
					character = PREV
				}
			}
			culture_group = germanic
			is_romanized_germanic_trigger = no
		}
		name = "EVTOPTD313032"
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				character = ROOT
				character = FROM
				event_target:linnius_liege = {
					character = PREV
				}
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { culture_group = germanic }
				is_romanized_germanic_trigger = yes
			}
			NOT = { trait = foederate_employer }
		}
		name = "EVTOPTC313032"
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				character = ROOT
				character = FROM
				event_target:linnius_liege = {
					character = PREV
				}
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { culture_group = germanic }
				is_romanized_germanic_trigger = yes
			}

# Ultimatum Refused
character_event = {
	id = 313034
	title = "EVTNAME313034"
	desc = "EVTDESC313034"
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_emissary"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313034"	# Go to war
		prestige = 200
		if = {
			limit = { independent = no }
			set_defacto_liege = THIS
		}
		if = {
			limit = { independent = yes }
			suzerain = {
				remove_tributary = ROOT
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = foederate_revolt
		set_character_flag = foederate_revolt_lindsey
		create_character = {
			random_traits = yes
			dynasty = random
			religion = germanic_pagan
			culture = angle
			female = no
			age = 30
			attributes = {
				martial = 10
			}
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
			trait = skilled_warrior
		}
		new_character = {
			spawn_unit = {
				province = 138 # Caistor
				troops =
				{
					light_infantry = { 1000 1000 }
					heavy_infantry = { 600 600 }
					pikemen = { 500 500 }
					archers = { 200 200 }
				}
				attrition = 1
			}
		}
		c_lindum = {
			reverse_war = {
				target = ROOT
				casus_belli = county_conquest
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {	id = 313036 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313034"	# Back down
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		prestige = -200
		FROM = {
			character_event = {	id = 313037 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

			has_character_flag = foederate_revolt_cantia
		}
		clr_character_flag = foederate_revolt_cantia
		prestige = 100
		if = {
			limit = { trait = foederate }
			remove_trait = foederate
		}
		d_cantware = { grant_title = ROOT }
		k_cantia = { grant_title = ROOT }
		46 = {
			remove_province_modifier = anglosaxon_settlement
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC313038"
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = foederate_revolt_bernicia
		}
		clr_character_flag = foederate_revolt_bernicia
		prestige = 100
		if = {
			limit = { trait = foederate }
			remove_trait = foederate
		}
		d_bernicia = { grant_title = ROOT }
		any_realm_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = anglosaxon_settlement }
			remove_province_modifier = anglosaxon_settlement
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD313038"
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = foederate_revolt_deira
		}
		clr_character_flag = foederate_revolt_deira
		prestige = 100
		if = {
			limit = { trait = foederate }
			remove_trait = foederate
		}
		d_deira = { grant_title = ROOT }
		any_realm_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = anglosaxon_settlement }
			remove_province_modifier = anglosaxon_settlement
		}
	}
}

# War ends - failure	
character_event = {
	id = 313039
	title = "EVTNAME313039"
	desc = "EVTDESC313039"
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_emissary"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = foederate_revolt
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313039"
		prestige = -200
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = foederate } }
			add_trait = foederate
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = foederate_revolt_lindsey }
			clr_character_flag = foederate_revolt_lindsey
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = lindsey_proper_liege }
				clr_character_flag = lindsey_proper_liege
				save_event_target_as = proper_liege
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = foederate_revolt_cantia }
			clr_character_flag = foederate_revolt_cantia
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = ceint_proper_liege }
				clr_character_flag = ceint_proper_liege
				save_event_target_as = proper_liege
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = foederate_revolt_bernicia }
			clr_character_flag = foederate_revolt_bernicia
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = bernicia_proper_liege }
				clr_character_flag = bernicia_proper_liege
				save_event_target_as = proper_liege
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = foederate_revolt_deira }
			clr_character_flag = foederate_revolt_deira
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = deira_proper_liege }
				clr_character_flag = deira_proper_liege
				save_event_target_as = proper_liege
			}
		}
		event_target:proper_liege = {
			reverse_imprison = ROOT
			make_tributary = { who = ROOT tributary_type = foederati }
		}
	}
}

	desc = "EVTDESC313040"
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_emissary"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

		clr_character_flag = foederate_revolt
		clr_character_flag = foederate_revolt_lindsey
		clr_character_flag = foederate_revolt_cantia
		clr_character_flag = foederate_revolt_bernicia
		clr_character_flag = foederate_revolt_deira
		any_character = {
			clr_character_flag = lindsey_proper_liege
			clr_character_flag = ceint_proper_liege
			clr_character_flag = bernicia_proper_liege
			clr_character_flag = deira_proper_liege
		}			
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313040"
		prestige = 50

			limit = { trait = foederate }
			remove_trait = foederate
		}
	}

# Clear settlements modifier if under duke level or higher
province_event = {
	id = 313041
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_modifier = anglosaxon_settlement
		OR = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
			owner = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						higher_real_tier_than = COUNT
						is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
						NOT = { trait = foederate }
					}
					liege = {
						higher_real_tier_than = COUNT
						is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
						NOT = { trait = foederate }
					}
					top_liege = {
						higher_real_tier_than = COUNT
						is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
						NOT = { trait = foederate }
					}
				}
				war = no
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}
	
	immediate = {
		remove_province_modifier = anglosaxon_settlement
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
	}
}

# Hengist of Portus Dubris give ultimatum
character_event = {
	id = 313080
	title = "EVTNAME313080"
	desc = "EVTDESC313080"
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_warships"
	
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_character_flag = angle_sending_ultimatum
			AND = {
				ai = yes		# Human player triggers by decision
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = ceint_pre_ultimatum
					e_britannia = {
						has_holder = no
					}
				}
				year = 452
				NOT = { year = 480 }
				war = no
				is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
				has_landed_title = c_thanet
				c_thanet = {
					location = {
						is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
						has_province_modifier = anglosaxon_settlement
					}
				}
				tier = count
				trait = foederate
				OR = {
					AND = {
						independent = no
						liege = {
							culture_group = celtic
						}
					}
					AND = {
						is_tributary = { type = foederati }
						suzerain = {
							culture_group = celtic
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = hengist_ceint_ultimatum }
					had_global_flag =  { flag = hengist_ceint_ultimatum days = 3650 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 120
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			year = 455
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			year = 460
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			year = 465
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			year = 470
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = angle_sending_ultimatum
		set_global_flag = hengist_ceint_ultimatum
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313080"	# Send Ultimatum
		ai_chance = { factor = 95 }
		if = {
			limit = { independent = no }
			liege = {
				character_event = {	id = 313081 days = 1 }
			}
			break = yes
		}
		suzerain = {
			character_event = {	id = 313081 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313080"	# Don't send ultimatum
		trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 5 
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = loyal }
					NOT = { trait = content }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					trait = unloyal
					trait = ambitious 
				}
			}
		}
		prestige = -100
	}
}

		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 80 
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				top_liege = {
					realm_size = 2
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				top_liege = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				top_liege = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				top_liege = {
					realm_size = 20
				}
			}
		}
		prestige = -200
		FROM = {
			character_event = {	id = 313082 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {

		prestige = 100
		FROM = {

		}

	}
}

# Ultimatum Accepted
character_event = {
	id = 313082
	title = "EVTNAME313082"
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_saxon_army_banners"
	
	major = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# Victorious Jutes
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313082
		trigger = {
			character = ROOT
		}
	}
	
	# Former ruler of Cantuaria
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313082_1
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
	}
	
	# Cantuaria liege, if there is one
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313082_2
		trigger = {
			event_target:cantuaria_liege = {
				character = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Other Anglo-Saxons
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313082_3
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				character = ROOT
				character = FROM
				event_target:cantuaria_liege = {
					character = PREV
				}
			}
			culture_group = germanic
			is_romanized_germanic_trigger = no
		}
	}
	
	# Other Britons
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313082_4
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				character = ROOT
				character = FROM
				event_target:cantuaria_liege = {
					character = PREV
				}
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { culture_group = germanic }
				is_romanized_germanic_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	major_trigger = {
		OR = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
			is_brythonic_culture_trigger = yes
			capital_scope = {
				region = world_britannia
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { independent = yes }
			suzerain = {
				save_event_target_as = former_liege
			}
			break = yes
		}
		liege = {
			save_event_target_as = former_liege
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313082"
		trigger = {
			character = ROOT
		}
		prestige = 200
		event_target:former_liege = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_landed_title = k_cantuaria
					num_of_king_titles = 1
					tier = KING
				}
				any_vassal = {
					limit = { tier = COUNT }
					set_character_flag = ceint_vassal
				}
				set_character_flag = ceint_vassal
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						num_of_king_titles = 2
						tier = EMPEROR
						NOT = { has_landed_title = k_cantuaria }
					}
				}
				any_province = {
					limit = { region = custom_cantware }
					county = {
						holder_scope = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									num_of_count_titles = 1
									tier = COUNT
									same_realm = FROM
								}
								set_character_flag = ceint_vassal
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = {
										OR = {
											num_of_count_titles = 1
											tier = COUNT
										}
									}
									same_realm = FROM
								}
								PREV = { grant_title = ROOT }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c_portus_dubris = {
					holder_scope = {
						same_realm = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			c_portus_dubris = {
				grant_title = ROOT
			}
		}
		d_cantware = { grant_title = ROOT }
		k_cantia = { grant_title = ROOT }
		d_cantuaria = { destroy_landed_title = d_cantuaria }
		k_cantuaria = { destroy_landed_title = k_cantuaria }
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = ceint_vassal }
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
			clr_character_flag = ceint_vassal
		}
		set_defacto_liege = THIS
		365 = {
			remove_province_modifier = anglosaxon_settlement
		}
		create_character = {
			random_traits = yes
			dynasty = random
			religion = germanic_pagan
			culture = jute
			female = no
			age = 30
			attributes = {
				martial = 10
			}
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
			trait = skilled_warrior
		}
		new_character = {
			spawn_unit = {
				province = 365 # Ynys Tanatus
				troops =
				{
					light_infantry = { 700 700 }
					heavy_infantry = { 300 300 }
					pikemen = { 200 200 }
				}
				attrition = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		name = "EVTOPTB313082"
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:cantuaria_liege = {
				character = PREV
			}
		}
		name = "EVTOPTC313082"
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				character = ROOT
				character = FROM
				event_target:cantuaria_liege = {
					character = PREV
				}
			}
			culture_group = germanic
			is_romanized_germanic_trigger = no
		}
		name = "EVTOPTD313082"
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				character = ROOT
				character = FROM
				event_target:cantuaria_liege = {
					character = PREV
				}
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { culture_group = germanic }
				is_romanized_germanic_trigger = yes
			}
			NOT = { trait = foederate_employer }
		}
		name = "EVTOPTC313082"
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				character = ROOT
				character = FROM
				event_target:cantuaria_liege = {
					character = PREV
				}
			}

# Ultimatum Refused
character_event = {
	id = 313084
	title = "EVTNAME313084"
	desc = "EVTDESC313084"
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_emissary"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313084"	# Go to war
		prestige = 200
		if = {
			limit = { independent = no }
			set_defacto_liege = THIS
		}
		if = {
			limit = { independent = yes }
			suzerain = {
				remove_tributary = ROOT
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = foederate_revolt
		set_character_flag = foederate_revolt_cantia
		create_character = {
			random_traits = yes
			dynasty = random
			religion = germanic_pagan
			culture = jute
			female = no
			age = 30
			attributes = {
				martial = 10
			}
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = veteran
			trait = brave
			trait = skilled_warrior
		}
		new_character = {
			spawn_unit = {
				province = 365 # Ynys Tanatus
				troops =
				{
					light_infantry = { 1000 1000 }
					heavy_infantry = { 600 600 }
					pikemen = { 500 500 }
				}
				attrition = 1
			}
		}
		c_portus_dubris = {
			reverse_war = {
				target = ROOT
				casus_belli = county_conquest
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {	id = 313086 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313084"	# Back down
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		prestige = -200
		FROM = {
			character_event = {	id = 313087 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

### COLLAPSE OF ANGLIA ###

# On-action "bounce" event (death)
character_event = {
	id = 313100
	desc = "EVTDESC313101"
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		character = 80
		OR = {
			has_landed_title = k_anglia
			has_landed_title = e_aengland
		}
		has_global_flag = aelle_ruling_anglia
	}
	
	immediate = {
		k_anglia = {
			current_heir = {
				character_event = { id = 313101 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
	}
}

# Death of Aelle
narrative_event = {
	id = 313101
	title = "EVTNAME313101"
	desc = "EVTDESC313101"
	major = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = anglia_collapse_start
		clr_global_flag = aelle_ruling_anglia
		#k_anglia = {
		#	holder_scope = {
		#		set_character_flag = anglia_collapse_target
		#	}
		#}
		d_cilternsaete = { de_jure_liege = k_mercia }
		d_middle_angles = { de_jure_liege = k_mercia }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313101"
		trigger = {
			has_landed_title = k_anglia
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = anglia_unstable_realm
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313101"
		trigger = {
			any_liege = {
				has_landed_title = k_anglia
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC313101"
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					any_liege = {
						has_landed_title = k_anglia
					}
					has_landed_title = k_anglia
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD313101"
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_liege = {
					has_landed_title = k_anglia
				}
			}
			OR = {
				culture = briton
				culture = romanobritish
				culture = cumbrian
				culture_group = imperiale
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTE313101"
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
					culture = briton
					culture = romanobritish
					culture = cumbrian
					culture_group = imperiale
					any_liege = {
						has_landed_title = k_anglia
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# "Bounce" event (deposition)
character_event = {
	id = 313102
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 15
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = aelle_ruling_anglia
		character = 80
		NOR = {
			has_landed_title = k_anglia
			has_landed_title = e_aengland
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		k_anglia = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = { id = 313103 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
	}
}

# King informed of vassals scheming
character_event = {
	id = 313104
	desc = "EVTDESC313104"
	picture = "GFX_evt_hall_long_lady"
	
	only_rulers = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = anglia_collapse_start
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = anglia_collapse_factions }
			had_global_flag = { flag = anglia_collapse_factions days = 1825 }
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = anglia_first_revolt }
			had_global_flag = { flag = anglia_first_revolt days = 1825 }
		}
		#has_character_flag = anglia_collapse_target
		NOT = { has_global_flag = anglia_collapsed }
		has_landed_title = k_anglia
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = anglia_collapse_factions
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = { 
					higher_tier_than = BARON 
					#NOT = { trait = incapable }	
					#is_adult = yes
					prisoner = no
				}
				character_event = { id = 313105 days = 30 random = 10 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313104"
		prestige = -50
	}
}

# Vassals join independence faction
character_event = {
	id = 313105
	desc = "EVTDESC313105"
	picture = "GFX_evt_castle_rider_arriving"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313105"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				OR = {
					trait = ambitious
					trait = unloyal
				}
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = anglia_collapse_faction
		prestige = 50
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { in_faction = faction_independence } }
				leave_faction = all
			}
		}
		start_faction = {
			faction = faction_independence
			can_join_existing = yes
			ignore_requirements = yes
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { in_faction = faction_independence } }
				liege = {
					any_vassal = {
						limit = { leads_faction = faction_independence }
						ROOT = {
							join_faction = {
								faction = faction_independence
								faction_leader = PREV
								#ignore_requirements = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313105"
		prestige = -50
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 5		
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						trait = content
						trait = loyal
						liege = {
							reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 80 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				in_faction = faction_independence
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				liege = {
					reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				AND = {
					trait = content
					trait = loyal
				}
			}			
		}
	}
}

# Force faction ultimatum if AI takes too long
character_event = {
	id = 3131051
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	picture = "GFX_evt_castle_rider_arriving"
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	ai = yes
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 15
	
	trigger = {
		had_character_flag = { flag = anglia_collapse_faction days = 20 }
		leads_faction = faction_independence
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			letter_event = { id = 8035 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8005" }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_character_flag = faction_independence_ultimatum_taken
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "OK"
	}
}
		
# Revolting vassals get event troops
character_event = {
	id = 313106
	desc = "EVTDESC313106"
	picture = "GFX_evt_saxon_army"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313106"
		location = {
			ROOT = {
				spawn_unit = {
					province = PREV
					home = PREV
					owner = ROOT
					troops = {
						pikemen = { 900 900 }
						heavy_infantry = { 900 900 }
						archers = { 800 800 }
						light_infantry = { 1200 1200 }
						light_cavalry = { 200 200 }
					}
					attrition = 0.1
					disband_on_peace = yes
				}
				spawn_unit = {
					province = PREV
					home = PREV
					owner = ROOT
					troops = {
						pikemen = { 600 600 }
						heavy_infantry = { 600 600 }
						archers = { 500 500 }
						light_infantry = { 800 800 }
					}
					attrition = 0.1
					disband_on_peace = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Successful revolt - Anglia dissolves
narrative_event = {
	id = 313107
	title = "EVTNAME313107"
	desc = "EVTDESC313107"
	major = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_burning_fire"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_eastseaxe = { de_jure_liege = k_eastseaxe }
		d_middleseaxe = { de_jure_liege = k_eastseaxe }
		d_grentbryce = { de_jure_liege = k_mercia }
		d_middle_angles = { de_jure_liege = k_mercia }
		d_cilternsaete = { de_jure_liege = k_mercia }
		d_norfolc = { de_jure_liege = k_east_anglia }
		d_southfolc = { de_jure_liege = k_east_anglia }
		
		set_global_flag = anglia_collapsed
		clr_global_flag = anglia_collapse_factions
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313107"
		trigger = {
			has_landed_title = k_anglia
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = anglia_unstable_realm }
			remove_character_modifier = anglia_unstable_realm
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = anglia_unstable_realm_2 }
			remove_character_modifier = anglia_unstable_realm_2
		}
		k_anglia = { 
			destroy_landed_title = THIS
			activate_title = { title = THIS status = no }
		}
		prestige = -200
		any_vassal = {
			limit = { 
				higher_tier_than = BARON 
				OR = {
					higher_tier_than = COUNT
					NOT = {
						primary_title = {
							duchy = {
								holder_scope = {
									character = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_defacto_liege = THIS
		}
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				suzerain = { character = ROOT }
			}
			ROOT = { remove_tributary = PREV }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			k_east_anglia = { 
				activate_title = { title = THIS status = yes }
				#insert_title_history = k_anglia
			}
			#add_pressed_claim = k_anglia
			#clr_character_flag = anglia_collapse_target
			# if = {
				# limit = {
					# NOT = { has_landed_title = d_middleseaxe }
					# d_middleseaxe = { has_holder = yes }
				# }
				# add_pressed_claim = d_middleseaxe
			# }
			any_war = {
				limit = {
					attacker = { character = ROOT }
				}
				end_war = invalid
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313107"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				liege = {
					has_landed_title = k_anglia
				}
				has_character_flag = anglia_collapse_faction
			}
			NOT = { has_landed_title = k_anglia }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			clr_character_flag = anglia_collapse_faction
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC313107"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture = briton
				culture = romanobritish
				culture = cumbrian
				culture_group = imperiale
			}
			NOR = {
				liege = {
					has_landed_title = k_anglia
				}
				has_character_flag = anglia_collapse_faction
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD313107"
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				OR = {
					culture = briton
					culture = romanobritish
					culture = cumbrian
					culture_group = imperiale
				}
				OR = {
					liege = {
						has_landed_title = k_anglia
					}
					has_character_flag = anglia_collapse_faction
				}
				has_landed_title = k_anglia
			}
		}
	}
}

# Revolt Crushed
character_event = {
	id = 313110
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313110
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = anglia_first_revolt
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313110_1
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = anglia_first_revolt }
		}
	}
	picture = "GFX_evt_lord_overlooking_bridge"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_vassal = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = anglia_collapse_faction }
			character_event = { id = 313111 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313110"
		prestige = 200
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = anglia_first_revolt
		}
		remove_character_modifier = anglia_unstable_realm_2
		clr_global_flag = anglia_collapse_start
		clr_global_flag = anglia_collapse_factions
		any_character = {
			clr_character_flag = anglia_collapse_faction
			#clr_character_flag = anglia_collapse_target
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313110"
		prestige = 200
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = anglia_first_revolt }
		}
		set_global_flag = anglia_first_revolt
		remove_character_modifier = anglia_unstable_realm
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = anglia_unstable_realm_2
			duration = -1
		}
		any_character = {
			clr_character_flag = anglia_collapse_faction
			#clr_character_flag = anglia_collapse_target
		}
	}
}

# Maintenance event for anglia_unstable_realm modifier
character_event = {
	id = 313112
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	picture = "GFX_evt_lord_overlooking_bridge"
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				FROM = { title = k_anglia }
				has_global_flag = anglia_collapse_start
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_character_modifier = anglia_unstable_realm
					has_character_modifier = anglia_unstable_realm_2
				}
				NOT = { has_landed_title = k_anglia }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_landed_title = k_anglia }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = anglia_first_revolt }
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = anglia_unstable_realm_2
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = anglia_unstable_realm
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			FROMFROM = { remove_character_modifier = anglia_unstable_realm }
			FROMFROM = { remove_character_modifier = anglia_unstable_realm_2 }
		}
		else = {
			remove_character_modifier = anglia_unstable_realm
			remove_character_modifier = anglia_unstable_realm_2
		}
	}
}

### DECLINE OF SUSSEX ###

# Cerdic no longer rules Sussex
character_event = {
	id = 313090
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_landed_title = c_null
		has_global_flag = cerdic_ruling_sussex
		k_sussex = {
			OR = {
				has_holder = no			# This clears the flag but invalidates the event chain altogether
				holder_scope = { 
					NOR = { 
						character = 86 
						has_landed_title = e_aengland	# Won't get vassal revolts as Bretwalda
						AND = {			# Collapse of Anglia takes precedence, in case you somehow qualify for both
							has_landed_title = k_anglia
							has_global_flag = anglia_collapse_factions
						}
						independent = no	# Doesn't make sense to fragment while Sussex isn't independent
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_global_flag = cerdic_ruling_sussex
		k_sussex = { 
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_holder = yes
				}
				holder_scope = { character_event = { id = 313091 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Event for King of Sussex
character_event = {
	id = 313091
	title = "EVTNAME313091"
	desc = "EVTDESC313091"
	picture = "GFX_evt_storm_brewing"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = sussex_decline_start
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313091"
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = EVTOPTA313091TT
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = sussex_unstable_realm
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}

# 20 years pass - remove modifier

# No more potential revolting vassals - remove modifier
character_event = {
	id = 313094
	desc = "EVTDESC313094"
	picture = "GFX_evt_lord_overlooking_bridge"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_landed_title = k_sussex
		has_global_flag = sussex_decline_start
		NOT = {
			any_vassal = {
				culture_group = germanic
				higher_tier_than = BARON
				is_landed = yes
				NOR = {
					has_landed_title = d_the_weald
					primary_title = {
						tier = COUNT
						location = { region = custom_sussex }
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_landed_title = d_cantware
							has_landed_title = d_westcantware
							has_landed_title = d_surrey
							primary_title = {
								tier = COUNT
								location = { region = custom_cantia }
							}
						}
						ROOT = { has_landed_title = k_cantia }
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_landed_title = d_the_belgae
							has_landed_title = d_hampshire
							has_landed_title = d_berkshire
							has_landed_title = d_wiltshire
							has_landed_title = d_dorset
							has_landed_title = d_somerset
							has_landed_title = d_devon
							has_landed_title = d_cornwall
							primary_title = {
								tier = COUNT
								location = { region = custom_wessex }
							}
						}
						ROOT = { has_landed_title = k_wessex }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313094"
		remove_character_modifier = sussex_unstable_realm
		clr_global_flag = sussex_decline_start
	}
}

# Maintenance event for sussex_unstable_realm modifier
character_event = {
	id = 313095
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	picture = "GFX_evt_lord_overlooking_bridge"
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				FROM = { title = k_sussex }
				has_global_flag = sussex_decline_start
			}
			AND = {
				has_character_modifier = sussex_unstable_realm
				NOT = { has_landed_title = k_sussex }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_landed_title = k_sussex }
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = sussex_unstable_realm
				duration = -1
			}
			FROMFROM = { remove_character_modifier = sussex_unstable_realm }
		}
		else = {
			remove_character_modifier = sussex_unstable_realm
		}
	}
}

# RETURN OF THE SAXONS

# Create warlord title
character_event = {
	id = 313150
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	picture = GFX_evt_lord_overlooking_bridge
	
	only_playable = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_landed_title = k_nuncio_britanniae
		had_global_flag = {
			flag = anglo_saxons_defeated
			days = 3650		# 10 years
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = anglo_saxon_return_title_created }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = anglo_saxon_return_title_created
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
				is_ruler = no
				is_heir = no
				is_adult = yes
				is_female = no
				NOT = { age = 50 }
				prisoner = no
				is_incapable = no
				OR = {
					any_claim = {
						capital_scope = { region = world_britannia }
					}
					any_title = {
						capital_scope = { region = world_britannia } 
						OR = {
							lower_tier_than = DUKE
							empire = { title = e_aengland }
						}
						any_previous_holder = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
			preferred_limit = {
				e_aengland = {		# Former Bretwalda
					any_previous_holder = {
						character = PREVPREV
					} 
				}
			}
			preferred_limit = {
				any_title = {		# Former King
					capital_scope = { region = world_britannia } 
					tier = KING
					empire = { title = e_aengland }
					any_previous_holder = {
						character = PREVPREV
					}
				}
			}
			preferred_limit = {
				any_claim = {		# Kingdom claimant
					capital_scope = { region = world_britannia } 
					tier = KING
					empire = { title = e_aengland }
				}
			}
			preferred_limit = {
				any_title = {		# Former Duke
					capital_scope = { region = world_britannia } 
					tier = DUKE
					empire = { title = e_aengland }
					any_previous_holder = {
						character = PREVPREV
					}
				}
			}
			preferred_limit = {
				any_claim = {		# Duchy claimant
					capital_scope = { region = world_britannia } 
					tier = DUKE
					empire = { title = e_aengland }
				}
			}
			preferred_limit = {
				any_title = {		# Former Count
					capital_scope = { region = world_britannia } 
					tier = COUNT
					any_previous_holder = {
						character = PREVPREV
					}
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = anglo_saxon_return_invader
			set_global_flag = anglo_saxon_return_invader_chosen
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = anglo_saxon_return_invader_chosen } }
			random_province = {
				limit = { 
					is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
					OR = {		# If somehow there are no Anglo-Saxon provinces in Britannia
						region = world_britannia
						NOT = { 
							any_province = {
								region = world_britannia
								is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
				create_character = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = random
					culture = THIS
					religion = THIS
					female = no
					age = 27
					attributes = {
						martial = 10
						diplomacy = 8
						intrigue = 7
					}
					trait = brilliant_strategist
					trait = veteran
					trait = brave
					trait = diligent
					trait = ambitious
				}
				new_character = {
					save_global_event_target_as = anglo_saxon_return_invader
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:anglo_saxon_return_invader = {
			create_title = {
				tier = DUKE
				holder = THIS
				landless = yes
				name = "ANGLO_SAXON_HOST_NAME"
				base_title = d_saxons
				ruler = HIGH_CHIEF
				foa = "HIGH_CHIEF_FOA"
				short_name = yes
			}
			new_title = {
				set_title_flag = anglo_saxon_return_invader_title
				save_global_event_target_as = anglo_saxon_return_invader_title_target
				adjective = ANGLO_SAXON_HOST_NAME_ADJ
				set_preferred_capital = 458	# Sturmaria			
			}
			prestige = 1000
			wealth = 250
			character_event = { id = 313151 }
		}
	}	
}

			# }
		# }
	# }
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC313152"	# Other Saxons
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes

# If the war invalidates, repeat the invasion
character_event = {
	id = 313153
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		# Invader gets some extra troops
		spawn_unit = {
			province = event_target:anglo_saxon_return_invader_target_province
			home = event_target:anglo_saxon_return_invader_target_province
			owner = THIS
			earmark = anglo_saxon_return_army
			troops = {
				light_infantry = { 500 500 }
				pikemen = { 400 400 }
				heavy_infantry = { 600 600 }
				archers = { 300 300 }
				light_cavalry = { 100 100 }
			}
			attrition = 0.25
			maintenance_multiplier = 0.25
		}
		event_target:anglo_saxon_return_invader_target_province = {
			kingdom = {
				event_target:anglo_saxon_return_invader = {
					unsafe_war = {
						casus_belli = full_kingdom_invasion
						target = PREVPREV
						thirdparty_title = PREVPREV
						tier = KING
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}


# Invasion victorious
narrative_event = {
	id = 313154
	title = "EVTNAME313154"
	desc = "EVTDESC313154"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_royal_court"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = anglo_saxons_returned_victorious
		if = {
			limit = { event_target:anglo_saxon_return_invader_target_province = { region = custom_eastanglia } }
			grant_title = k_east_anglia
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { event_target:anglo_saxon_return_invader_target_province = { region = custom_essex } }
			grant_title = k_eastseaxe
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { event_target:anglo_saxon_return_invader_target_province = { region = custom_cantia } }
			grant_title = k_cantia
		}
		set_character_flag = gained_aengland
		grant_title = e_aengland
		clr_character_flag = gained_aengland
		any_title = {
			limit = { has_title_flag = anglo_saxon_return_invader_title }
			activate_title = { title = THIS status = no }
			destroy_landed_title = THIS
		}
		clear_global_event_target = anglo_saxon_return_invader_title_target
		clear_global_event_target = anglo_saxon_return_invader
		
		# Force de jure duchy creation
		character_event = { id = 315003 days = 1 random = 3 }
		character_event = { id = 315003 days = 1 random = 3 }
		character_event = { id = 315003 days = 1 random = 3 }
		character_event = { id = 315003 days = 1 random = 3 }
		character_event = { id = 315003 days = 1 random = 3 }
		
		any_province = {
			limit = { 
				has_province_modifier = anglo_saxons_uprising
			}
			remove_province_modifier = anglo_saxons_uprising
		}
		set_character_flag = anglo_saxons_return_leader
		prestige = 750
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = great_leader_anglosaxon
			duration = -1
		}
		capital_scope = {
			ROOT = {
				spawn_unit = {
					province = PREV
					home = PREV
					owner = THIS
					earmark = anglo_saxon_return_army
					troops = {
						light_infantry = { 700 700 }
						pikemen = { 600 600 }
						heavy_infantry = { 1000 1000 }
						archers = { 450 450 }
						light_cavalry = { 100 100 }
					}
					attrition = 0.25
					maintenance_multiplier = 0.25
				}			
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313154"	# Saxons in Britannia
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
			capital_scope = {
				region = world_britannia
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = anglo_saxon_invasion_supporter }
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
		}
		clr_character_flag = anglo_saxon_invasion_supporter
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313154"	# Other Saxons
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
			NOT = {
				capital_scope = {
					region = world_britannia
				}
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = anglo_saxon_invasion_supporter
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC313154"	# Britons and British rulers
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_brythonic_culture_trigger = yes
				any_realm_province = {
					region = world_britannia
				}
			}
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_brythonic_culture_trigger = yes }
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = EVTOPTC313154TT
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD313154"	# Others
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
			NOR = {
				is_brythonic_culture_trigger = yes
				any_realm_province = {
					region = world_britannia
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	ai = yes

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				k_eastseaxe = {
					has_holder = no

				any_realm_province = {

# Anglo-Saxons defeated, 2.0
narrative_event = {
	id = 313158
	title = "EVTNAME313158"
	desc = {
		text = "EVTDESC313158"
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = anglo_saxons_returned_victorious
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC313158_1
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = anglo_saxons_returned_victorious }
		}
	}
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_people_captured"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_landed_title = k_nuncio_britanniae
			has_character_flag = defeated_anglo_saxon_return_leader
		}
		has_global_flag = anglo_saxons_defeated
		has_global_flag = anglo_saxons_returned
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				event_target:anglo_saxon_return_invader_title_target = {
					always = yes
				}
			}
			event_target:anglo_saxon_return_invader_title_target = {
				holder_scope = {
					OR = {
						war = no
						has_character_flag = defeated_anglo_saxon_return_leader
					}
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = anglo_saxons_defeated_again }
		NOT = {
			any_province = {
				region = world_britannia
				owner = {
					top_liege = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								culture_group = germanic
								is_romanized_germanic_trigger = no
							}
							primary_title = {
								higher_tier_than = COUNT
								OR = {
									title = e_aengland
									empire = { title = e_aengland }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = anglo_saxons_defeated_again
		any_title = {
			limit = { has_title_flag = anglo_saxon_return_invader_title }
			activate_title = { title = THIS status = no }
			destroy_landed_title = THIS
		}
		any_province = {
			limit = { 
				has_province_modifier = anglo_saxons_uprising
			}
			remove_province_modifier = anglo_saxons_uprising
		}
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				has_earmarked_regiments = anglo_saxon_return_army
			}
			disband_event_forces = anglo_saxon_return_army
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313158"	# Britons and British rulers
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_brythonic_culture_trigger = yes
				any_realm_province = {
					region = world_britannia
				}
			}
			NAND = {
				culture_group = germanic
				is_romanized_germanic_trigger = no
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313158"	# Saxons in Britannia
		trigger = {
			culture_group = germanic
			is_romanized_germanic_trigger = no
			capital_scope = {
				region = world_britannia
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC313158"	# Other Saxons
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
			NOT = {
				capital_scope = {
					region = world_britannia
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD313158"	# Norse
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				capital_scope = {
					region = world_britannia
				}
			}
			is_north_germanic_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTE313158"	# Others
		trigger = {
			is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = no
			is_north_germanic_trigger = no
			NOR = {
				is_brythonic_culture_trigger = yes
				any_realm_province = {
					region = world_britannia
				}
			}
		}

# REVOLTS FOR NEW ANGLOSAXON KINGDOMS
# Revolts for new Kingdoms - Mercia
character_event = {
	id = 313180
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 15
	prisoner = no
	capable_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		year = 600
		NOT = { year = 700 }
		ai = yes
		independent = no
		prisoner = no
		wealth = 20
		is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		NOT = { tier = KING }
		OR = { 
			has_landed_title = d_mercia
			has_landed_title = d_hwicce
			has_landed_title = d_magonsaete
			has_landed_title = d_tomsaete
			has_landed_title = d_wrocensaete
			has_landed_title = d_middle_angles
		}
		num_of_count_titles = 2
		NOT = { has_character_flag = revolt_for_mercia }
		top_liege = {
			NOT = { has_landed_title = k_mercia }
			NOT = { has_landed_title = e_aengland }
			NOT = {
				ROOT = { opinion = { who = PREV value = 75 } }
			}
			NAND = {
				has_landed_title = k_anglia
				has_global_flag = anglia_collapse_factions
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			k_mercia = { has_holder = yes }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		ROOT = {
			top_liege = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = bid_for_independence
				}
			}
		}
		add_claim = k_mercia
		add_trait = unloyal
		set_character_flag = revolt_for_mercia
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
		ROOT = {
			location = {
				ROOT = {
					spawn_unit = {
						province = PREV
						home = PREV
						owner = ROOT
						troops = {
							pikemen = { 800 800 }
							heavy_infantry = { 800 800 }
							archers = { 175 175 }
							light_infantry = { 400 400 }
						}
						attrition = 1
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								k_mercia = { any_previous_holder = { always = yes } }
							}
						}
						spawn_unit = {
							province = PREV
							home = PREV
							owner = ROOT
							troops = {
								pikemen = { 450 450 }
								heavy_infantry = { 650 650 }
								archers = { 125 125 }
								light_infantry = { 300 300 }
							}
							merge = yes
							attrition = 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
# Revolts for new Kingdoms - West Seaxe
character_event = {
	id = 313181
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 15
	prisoner = no
	capable_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		NOT = { year = 700 }
		independent = no
		prisoner = no
		wealth = 20
		is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		NOT = { tier = KING }
		OR = { 
			has_landed_title = d_dorset
			has_landed_title = d_hampshire
