			has_landed_title = d_somerset
		}
		num_of_count_titles = 2
		NOT = { has_character_flag = revolt_for_wessex }
		top_liege = {
			NOT = { has_landed_title = k_wessex }
			NOT = { has_landed_title = e_aengland }
			NOT = {
				ROOT = { opinion = { who = PREV value = 75 } }
			}
			NAND = {
				has_landed_title = k_anglia
				has_global_flag = anglia_collapse_factions
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			k_wessex = { has_holder = yes }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		ROOT = {
			liege = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = bid_for_independence
				}
			}
		}
		add_claim = k_wessex
		add_trait = unloyal
		set_character_flag = revolt_for_wessex
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
		ROOT = {
			location = {
				ROOT = {
					spawn_unit = {
						province = PREV
						home = PREV
						owner = ROOT
						troops = {
							pikemen = { 700 700 }
							heavy_infantry = { 600 600 }
							archers = { 175 175 }
						}
						attrition = 1
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								k_wessex = { any_previous_holder = { always = yes } }
							}
						}
						spawn_unit = {
							province = PREV
							home = PREV
							owner = ROOT
							troops = {
								pikemen = { 550 550 }
								heavy_infantry = { 450 450 }
								archers = { 125 125 }
							}
							merge = yes
							attrition = 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

# Generic Sussex vassal revolt
character_event = {
	id = 3131825
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 15
	prisoner = no
	capable_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		is_landed = yes
		independent = no
		prisoner = no
		wealth = 5
		culture_group = germanic
		higher_tier_than = BARON
		NOT = { tier = KING }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = revolt_from_sussex }
		liege = {
			has_landed_title = k_sussex
			NOT = { has_landed_title = k_wessex }
			NOT = { has_landed_title = e_aengland }
			NOT = {
				ROOT = { opinion = { who = PREV value = 75 } }
			}
			has_character_modifier = sussex_unstable_realm
			independent = yes
		}
		NOR = {
			has_landed_title = d_cantware
			has_landed_title = d_westcantware
			has_landed_title = d_the_weald
			has_landed_title = d_the_belgae
			primary_title = {
				tier = COUNT
				location = {
					OR = {
						region = custom_sussex
						region = custom_cantware
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 60
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = cantia_created
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = meonware_conquered }
				d_the_belgae = {
					holder_scope = {
						OR = {
							independent = yes
							top_liege = {
								has_landed_title = k_sussex
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		ROOT = {
			top_liege = {
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = bid_for_independence
				}
			}
		}
		add_trait = unloyal
		set_character_flag = revolt_from_sussex
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
		ROOT = {
			location = {
				ROOT = {
					spawn_unit = {
						province = PREV
						home = PREV
						owner = ROOT
						troops = {
							light_infantry = { 300 300 }
							pikemen = { 500 500 }
							heavy_infantry = { 450 450 }
							archers = { 250 250 }
						}
						attrition = 0.5
					}
					spawn_unit = {
						province = PREV
						home = PREV
						owner = ROOT
						earmark = sussex_revolt_troops
						troops = {
							light_infantry = { 300 300 }
							pikemen = { 500 500 }
							heavy_infantry = { 450 450 }
							archers = { 250 250 }
						}
						disband_on_peace = yes
						attrition = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		OR = {
			has_landed_title = k_anglia
			has_landed_title = k_sussex
		}
		NOT = { has_landed_title = d_middleseaxe }
		has_landed_title = c_verulanium
		any_vassal = {
			has_landed_title = d_middleseaxe
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
		any_vassal = {
			limit = {
				has_landed_title = d_middleseaxe
			}
			c_verulanium = {
				grant_title = PREV
			}
		}
	}
}
province_event = {		# Generic province-granting event for Anglia or Sussex
	id = 313171
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	
	trigger = {
		owner = {
			ai = yes
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_landed_title = k_anglia
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = aelle_ruling_anglia
						has_global_flag = anglia_collapse_start
					}
					NOT = { has_global_flag = anglia_collapsed }
				}
				AND = {
					has_landed_title = k_sussex
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = cerdic_ruling_sussex
						has_global_flag = sussex_decline_start
					}
				}
			}
			NOR = {
				AND = {
					has_landed_title = k_anglia
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							region = custom_essex
							region = custom_eastanglia
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_landed_title = k_sussex
					ROOT = {
						region = custom_sussex
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = { num_of_king_titles = 2 }
			num_of_count_titles = 2
			#any_courtier = {
			#	ai = yes
			#	age = 20
			#	is_female = no
			#	culture = PREV
			#	is_ruler = no
			#	NOT = { dynasty = PREV }
			#}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 6
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.01
			owner = {
				has_landed_title = k_anglia
				NOT = { has_character_flag = aelle_of_anglia }
			}
			has_global_flag = anglia_collapse_start
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.01
			owner = {
				has_character_modifier = sussex_unstable_realm
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = anglo_saxon_forced_grant
		if = {				# Try to grant to existing count in Middle Anglia
			limit = {
				region = custom_middleanglia
				d_middle_angles = { has_holder = no }
				owner = {
					ROOT = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							region = custom_middleanglia
							owner = {
								tier = COUNT
								culture = PREVPREVPREV
								same_realm = PREVPREVPREV
								NOT = { num_of_count_titles = 3 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					owner = {
						ROOT = {
							random_neighbor_province = {
								limit = {
									region = custom_middleanglia
									owner = {
										tier = COUNT
										culture = PREVPREVPREV
										same_realm = PREVPREVPREV
										NOT = { num_of_count_titles = 3 }
									}
								}
								owner = {
									ROOT = {
										county = {
											grant_title = PREVPREV
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					break = yes
				}
				50 = {
				}
			}
		}
		if = {				# Try to grant to existing count in Cilternsaete
			limit = {
				region = custom_cilternsaete
				d_cilternsaete = { has_holder = no }
				owner = {
					ROOT = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							region = custom_cilternsaete
							owner = {
								tier = COUNT
								culture = PREVPREVPREV
								same_realm = PREVPREVPREV
								NOT = { num_of_count_titles = 3 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					owner = {
						ROOT = {
							random_neighbor_province = {
								limit = {
									region = custom_cilternsaete
									owner = {
										tier = COUNT
										culture = PREVPREVPREV
										same_realm = PREVPREVPREV
										NOT = { num_of_count_titles = 3 }
									}
								}
								owner = {
									ROOT = {
										county = {
											grant_title = PREVPREV
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					break = yes
				}
				50 = {
				}
			}
		}
		if = {						# Grant to courtier (default option)
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					duchy = {
						has_holder = yes
						holder_scope = {
							ROOT = {
								owner = {
									same_realm = PREVPREV
									NOT = { character = PREVPREV }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				random_courtier = {
					limit = {
						ai = yes
						age = 20
						is_female = no
						culture = PREV
						is_ruler = no
						NOT = { dynasty = PREV }
					}
					ROOT = {
						county = {
							grant_title = PREVPREV
						}
					}
					prestige = 250
					wealth = 100
					break = yes
				}
				create_character = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = random
					religion = THIS
					culture = THIS
					female = no
					age = 25
					attributes = {
						diplomacy = 9
						martial = 7
					}
				}
				new_character = {
					ROOT = {
						county = {
							grant_title = PREVPREV
						}
					}
					prestige = 250
					wealth = 100
				}
				break = yes
			}
		}
		random_list = {						# Grant to duchy holder or make a vassal for him
			50 = {
				owner = {
					random_courtier = {
						limit = {
							ai = yes
							age = 20
							is_female = no
							culture = PREV
							is_ruler = no
							NOT = { dynasty = PREV }
						}
						ROOT = {
							county = {
								grant_title = PREVPREV
							}
						}
						prestige = 150
						wealth = 75
						ROOT = {
							duchy = {
								holder_scope = {
									set_defacto_vassal = PREVPREVPREV
								}
							}
						}
						break = yes
					}
					create_character = {
						random_traits = yes
						dynasty = random
						religion = THIS
						culture = THIS
						female = no
						age = 25
						attributes = {
							diplomacy = 9
							martial = 7
						}
					}
					new_character = {
						ROOT = {
							county = {
								grant_title = PREVPREV
							}
						}
						prestige = 150
						wealth = 75
						ROOT = {
							duchy = {
								holder_scope = {
									set_defacto_vassal = PREVPREVPREV
								}
							}
						}
					}
					break = yes
				}
			}
			50 = {
				duchy = {
					holder_scope = {
						ROOT = {
							county = {
								grant_title = PREVPREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
	}
}
character_event = {		# Generic duchy-granting event for Anglia or Sussex
	id = 313172
	desc = "You're not supposed to see this..."
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		OR = {
			has_landed_title = k_sussex
			has_landed_title = k_anglia
		}
		any_demesne_title = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					title = d_the_weald
					title = d_eastseaxe
					title = d_middleseaxe
					title = d_norfolc
					title = d_southfolc
				}
			}
			tier = DUKE
		}
		num_of_duke_titles = 2
		NOT = { year = 540 }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		any_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						title = d_the_weald
						title = d_eastseaxe
						title = d_middleseaxe
						title = d_norfolc
						title = d_southfolc
					}
				}
				tier = DUKE
			}
			any_direct_de_jure_vassal_title = {
				limit = {
					holder_scope = {
						top_liege = {
							character = ROOT
						}
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
						tier = COUNT
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							has_landed_title = PREVPREV
						}
					}
					holder_scope = {
						grant_title = PREVPREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "OK"
	}
}

# Conquest of Magnis - Roman Fort Destroyed
narrative_event = {
	id = 313179
	title = "EVTNAME313179"
	desc = "EVTDESC313179"
	picture = "GFX_evt_siege"
	
	major = no
	hide_new = yes
	only_rulers = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = magnis_fort_destroyed }
		is_ingvaeonic_culture_trigger = yes
		has_landed_title = c_magnis
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = magnis_fort_destroyed
		22 = {
			set_province_flag = magnis_fort_destroyed
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313179"
	}
}

character_event = {			# House of West Seaxe
	id = 313197
	title = "EVTNAME313197"
	desc = "EVTDESC313197"
	major = yes
	hide_new = yes

	picture = "GFX_evt_castle_hill"
	
	only_rulers = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		NOR = { 
			has_global_flag = wessex_house
			had_global_flag = { flag = wessex_created days = 60 }
			dynasty = 816
			num_of_king_titles = 2
		}
		has_landed_title = k_wessex
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = wessex_house
		ROOT = {
			dynasty = 333
			any_child = {
				dynasty = 333
				any_child = {
					dynasty = 333
					any_child = {
						dynasty = 333
						any_child = {
							dynasty = 333
						}
					}
				}
			}
			father_even_if_dead = {
				any_child = {
					limit = {
						is_ruler = no
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = 60 }
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 40 }
					}
					dynasty = 333
					any_child = {
						limit = { is_ruler = no }
						dynasty = 333
						any_child = {
							limit = { is_ruler = no }
							dynasty = 333
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA313197"
		trigger = {
			dynasty = 333
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB313197"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { dynasty = 333 }
		}
	}
}
